## 加油
---
## to make an extra effort; to cheer someone on
### jiāyóu
---
- **definition:** to make an extra effort; to cheer someone on
- **pinyin:** jiāyóu
- **components:**
  - 加
    - jiā
    - add; increase; join
  - 油
    - yóu
    - oil; fuel; grease
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 加 (jiā, "add") + 油 (yóu, "oil") - in racing contexts, to add oil originally referred to adding fuel for more power, hence cheering someone on to do better.
  - **interpretation:** 加油 (jiāyóu) literally means 'add oil,' a metaphorical expression encouraging someone to work harder, persevere, or do better. Historically, the term derived from motor sports where adding oil meant boosting vehicle performance, thus symbolically encouraging someone to enhance their efforts.
- **examples:**
  - 比( )赛(賽)前( )，教( )练(練)对(對)运(運)动(動)员(員)说(說)要( )加( )油( )。
    - Bǐsài qián, jiàoliàn duì yùndòngyuán shuō yào jiāyóu.
    - Before the match, the coach told the athletes to make an extra effort.
  - 考( )试(試)时(時)，同( )学(學)互( )相( )加( )油( )。
    - Kǎoshì shí, tóngxué hùxiāng jiāyóu.
    - During the exam, classmates cheered each other on.
  - 比( )赛(賽)中( )，观(觀)众(眾)不( )断(斷)喊( )加( )油( )。
    - Bǐsài zhōng, guānzhòng bùduàn hǎn jiāyóu.
    - During the competition, the audience continuously shouted encouragement.
### 加油 → 加
- **definition:** add; increase; join
- **pinyin:** jiā
- **components:**
  - 力
    - lì
    - strength
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 力 (lì, "strength") + 口 (kǒu, "mouth") ->
    - exertion with additional effort or breath ->
    - add
  - **interpretation:** The character 加 (jiā, "add") combines 力 (lì, "strength"), indicating physical effort or force, with 口 (kǒu, "mouth"), suggesting either verbal command or the exertion of breath when effort is applied. This combination evokes the image of putting in more effort, hence the meaning "add" as in adding effort or increasing in quantity. The evolution from the effortful action to 'add' bridges the concept of augmenting or increasing.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)在( )茶( )里(裡)加( )些( )糖( )。
    - Qǐng zài chá lǐ jiā xiē táng.
    - Please add some sugar to the tea.
  - 你( )可( )以( )加( )我( )为(為)好( )友( )吗？
    - Nǐ kěyǐ jiā wǒ wéi hǎoyǒu ma?
    - Can you add me as a friend?
  - 我( )们(們)需( )要( )加( )倍( )努( )力( )，才( )能( )完( )成( )这(這)个(個)项(項)目( )。
    - Wǒmen xūyào jiābèi nǔlì, cái néng wánchéng zhège xiàngmù.
    - We need to double our efforts in order to complete this project.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 加](@media/glyph52a0.png)
### 加油 → 加 → 力
- **definition:** strength
- **pinyin:** lì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts either an arm bending out from the side of the body, or a wooden plough
  - **interpretation:** The character 力(lì, 'strength') visually represents physical power through the image of an arm or tool, emphasizing the fundamental concept of muscular force.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )尽(盡)全( )力( )，赢(贏)得( )比( )赛(賽)。
    - Tā yòng jìn quánlì, yíng dé bǐsài.
    - He used all his strength to win the competition.
  - 他( )把( )力( )气(氣)用( )在( )学(學)习(習)上( )。
    - Tā bǎ lìqì yòng zài xuéxí shàng.
    - He applies his strength to his studies.
  - 面( )对(對)困( )难(難)，他( )毫( )不( )退( )缩(縮)，全力以赴。
    - Miànduì kùnnán, tā háo bù tuìsuō, quánlì yǐ fù.
    - Facing difficulties, he neither retreats nor gives up, but goes all out.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 力](@media/glyph529b.png)
### 加油 → 加 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 加油 → 油
- **definition:** oil; fuel; grease
- **pinyin:** yóu
- **components:**
  - 氵
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 由
    - yóu
    - reason
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 氵 (shuǐ, 'water') + phonetic 由 (yóu, 'reason') =
    - liquid that flows ->
    - oil, sauce
  - **interpretation:** The character 油(yóu) combines the water radical 氵 (shuǐ, 'water') with the phonetic 由 (yóu, 'reason'). This suggests something liquid, aligning with the meanings 'oil' and 'sauce', both of which flow like water.
- **examples:**
  - 油( )可( )以( )用( )来(來)炒( )菜( )。
    - Yóu kěyǐ yòng lái chǎo cài.
    - Oil can be used for stir-frying dishes.
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)辣( )椒( )油( )，因( )为(為)它( )增( )加( )了( )味( )道( )。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān làjiāo yóu, yīnwèi tā zēngjiāle wèidào.
    - I like chili oil because it enhances the flavor.
  - 煎( )鱼(魚)时(時)可( )以( )先( )在( )鱼(魚)上( )抹( )点(點)油( )，这(這)样(樣)鱼(魚)更( )滑( )嫩( )。
    - Jiān yú shí kěyǐ xiān zài yú shàng mǒ diǎn yóu, zhèyàng yú gèng huá nèn.
    - When pan-frying fish, you can first spread a little oil on the fish, so that the fish becomes more tender.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 油](@media/glyph6cb9.png)
### 加油 → 油 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字( )中( )偏( )旁( )氵( )，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快( )戏(戲)水( )。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 加油 → 油 → 由
- **definition:** reason
- **pinyin:** yóu
- **components:**
  - 十
    - shí
    - ten
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic 十 (needle) + semantic 口 (mouth) ->
    - container with a needle symbolizing an ancient pronunciation
  - **interpretation:** The character 由(yóu, 'cause') depicts a container with a top resembling a needle (十), phonetic for sound with 口 (mouth) for semantic influence, symbolizing something that originates from a cause, just as contents originate from a container.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)问(問)题(題)由( )他( )负(負)责(責)。
    - Zhège wèntí yóu tā fùzé.
    - This issue is caused by him to be responsible.
  - 一( )切( )的( )变(變)化( )都( )是( )由( )时(時)间(間)引( )起( )的( )。
    - Yīqiè de biànhuà dōu shì yóu shíjiān yǐnqǐ de.
    - All changes are caused by the passage of time.
  - 胜(勝)利( )由( )努( )力( )而( )来(來)。
    - Shènglì yóu nǔlì ér lái.
    - Victory is caused by effort.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 由](@media/glyph7531.png)
### 加油 → 油 → 由 → 十
- **definition:** ten
- **pinyin:** shí
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original vertical stroke ->
    - later horizontal stroke added ->
    - forms a cross ->
    - represents 'ten'
  - **interpretation:** The character 十(shí, 'ten') represents the number ten with a cross shape that could be seen as tally marks. It evolved from a simple vertical stroke to a cross by adding a horizontal stroke, symbolizing a complete set of ten.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )十( )本( )书(書)。
    - Wǒ yǒu shí běn shū.
    - I have ten books.
  - 花( )园(園)里(裡)有( )十( )棵( )树(樹)，景( )色( )十( )分( )优(優)美( )。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu shí kē shù, jǐngsè shífēn yōuměi.
    - There are ten trees in the garden, and the scenery is very beautiful.
  - 十( )年( )磨( )一( )剑(劍)。
    - Shí nián mó yī jiàn.
    - It takes ten years of practice to hone a sword.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 十](@media/glyph5341.png)
### 加油 → 油 → 由 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

## 雪
---
## snow
### xuě
---
- **definition:** snow
- **pinyin:** xuě
- **components:**
  - 雨
    - yǔ
    - rain
  - 彗
    - huì
    - broom
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 雨 (yǔ, "rain") + phonetic 彗 (huì, "broom") ->
    - snow
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 雨 (yǔ, "rain") for the semantic idea of precipitation and 彗 (huì, "broom") for its phonetic value. The image of rain light and fluffy as a broom sweep implies the specific type of precipitation: snow.
- **examples:**
  - 冬( )天( )的( )时(時)候( )，我( )们(們)经(經)常( )去( )山( )上( )滑( )雪( )。
    - Dōngtiān de shíhòu, wǒmen jīngcháng qù shānshàng huáxuě.
    - In winter, we often go to the mountains to ski.
  - 昨天晚上下了很多雪。
    - Zuótiān wǎnshàng xiàle hěnduō xuě.
    - It snowed a lot last night.
  - 雪( )花( )在( )阳(陽)光( )下( )闪(閃)闪(閃)发(發)光( )。
    - Xuěhuā zài yángguāng xià shǎnshǎn fāguāng.
    - The snowflakes sparkle under the sunlight.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 雪](@media/glyph96ea.png)
### 雪 → 雨
- **definition:** rain
- **pinyin:** yǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a cloud with drops of rain falling from it ->
    - horizontal stroke added later ->
    - rain
  - **interpretation:** 雨 (yǔ, "rain") visually represents rain falling from a cloud, capturing its essential form.
- **examples:**
  - 今天雨下得很大。
    - Jīntiān yǔ xià de hěn dà.
    - It rained hard today.
  - 他( )忘( )记(記)带(帶)伞(傘)，雨( )却(卻)毫( )不( )留( )情( )。
    - Tā wàngjì dài sǎn, yǔ què háobù liúqíng.
    - He forgot to bring an umbrella, and the rain showed no mercy.
  - 细(細)雨( )如( )丝(絲)，轻(輕)拂( )着(著)花( )瓣( )。
    - Xì yǔ rú sī, qīng fú zhe huā bàn.
    - The fine rain falls like silk, gently brushing the petals.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 雨](@media/glyph96e8.png)
### 雪 → 彗
- **definition:** broom
- **pinyin:** huì
- **components:**
  - 甡
    - shēn
    - broom
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 甡 (shēn, "broom") + 又 (yòu, "hand") =
    - holding a broom
  - **interpretation:** The character 彗 (huì, "broom") combines 甡 (shēn, "broom") with 又 (yòu, "hand") to depict the action of holding a broom. This emphasizes the function and use of a broom, suggesting an object specifically designed to be held by hand for sweeping.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )拿( )着(著)破( )旧(舊)的( )彗( )，清( )扫(掃)庭( )院( )。
    - Tā ná zhe pò jiù de huì, qīng sǎo tíng yuàn.
    - He holds the old broom and sweeps the courtyard.
  - 老匠人用彗，细(細)致(緻)打( )扫(掃)作( )坊( )。
    - Lǎo jiàngrén yòng huì, xìzhì dǎsǎo zuòfāng.
    - The old craftsman uses the broom to meticulously clean the workshop.
  - 在寒冬夜晚，他默默拿起彗，清( )扫(掃)门(門)前( )。
    - Zài hán dōng yè wǎn, tā mò mò ná qǐ huì, qīng sǎo mén qián.
    - On a cold winter night, he silently picked up the broom and swept the front door.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 彗](@media/glyph5f57.png)
### 雪 → 彗 → 甡
- **definition:** broom
- **pinyin:** shēn
- **components:**
  - 生
    - shēng
    - life
  - 辛
    - xīn
    - bitter; toilsome
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 生 (shēng, "life") + phonetic 辛 (xīn) ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** The character 甡 contains the semantic component 生 (shēng, "life") which may suggest something related to production or generation, combined with the phonetic 辛 (xīn), which contributes the sound. The character's connection to 'broom' is through borrowing for phonetic purposes and does not derive directly from its parts.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 甡](@media/glyph7521.png)
### 雪 → 彗 → 甡 → 生
- **definition:** life
- **pinyin:** shēng
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 屮 (chè, "sprout") on top of a horizontal line ->
    - signifies a plant sprouting from the ground ->
    - symbolizes life
  - **interpretation:** The character 生 (shēng, "life") represents the concept of life force or vitality, symbolized by a sprout emerging from the earth, embodying growth and renewal.
- **examples:**
  - 生( )命( )是( )一( )场(場)美( )丽(麗)的( )旅( )程( )。
    - Shēngmìng shì yī chǎng měilì de lǚchéng.
    - Life is a beautiful journey.
  - 他( )在( )战(戰)场(場)上( )奋(奮)力( )生( )存( )。
    - Tā zài zhànchǎng shàng fènlì shēngcún.
    - He fights to live on the battlefield.
  - 这(這)家( )餐( )厅(廳)的( )生( )鱼(魚)片( )非( )常( )新( )鲜(鮮)。
    - Zhè jiā cāntīng de shēngyúpiàn fēicháng xīnxiān.
    - The raw fish slices at this restaurant are very fresh.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 生](@media/glyph751f.png)
### 雪 → 彗 → 甡 → 生 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春( )雨( )滋( )润(潤)后(後)，小( )屮( )冲(沖)破( )泥( )土( )而( )出( )。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 屮](@media/glyph5c6e.png)
### 雪 → 彗 → 甡 → 辛
- **definition:** bitter; toilsome
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a tool—chisel or awl—used to mark slaves and criminals ->
    - 辛
  - **interpretation:** The character 辛 (xīn) originally depicted a tool such as a chisel, used for marking or branding. The association with a sharp tool helps explain its extended meaning of 'spice,' as spices can have a pungent, sharp quality reminiscent of a tool's point or effect.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)菜( )有( )一( )种(種)辛( )辣( )的( )味( )道( )。
    - Zhège cài yǒu yī zhǒng xīnlà de wèidào.
    - This dish has a spicy taste.
  - 他( )喜( )欢(歡)在( )食( )物( )里(裡)添( )加( )辛( )香( )料( )。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài shíwù lǐ tiānjiā xīn xiāngliào.
    - He likes to add spices to the food.
  - 这(這)种(種)辛( )口( )的( )调(調)料( )非( )常( )受( )欢(歡)迎( )。
    - Zhè zhǒng xīnkǒu de tiáoliào fēicháng shòu huānyíng.
    - This type of spicy seasoning is very popular.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 辛](@media/glyph8f9b.png)
### 雪 → 彗 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又( )」这(這)个(個)字( )最( )早( )来(來)源( )于(於)手( )。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很( )多( )汉(漢)字( )含( )有( )又( )部( )首( )，表( )示( )与(與)手( )有( )关(關)的( )动(動)作( )。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古( )人( )用( )又( )描( )绘(繪)手( )的( )形( )态(態)，体(體)现(現)了( )古( )汉(漢)字( )的( )独(獨)特( )魅( )力( )。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)

## 零下
---
## zero; below zero
### líng (xià)
---
- **definition:** zero; below zero
- **pinyin:** líng (xià)
- **components:**
  - 零
    - líng
    - zero; nil; fragment; fractional
  - 下
    - xià
    - below; under; next; to descend
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 零 (líng, "zero") refers to the numerical value of zero, representing the absence of quantity. 下 (xià, "below") indicates a position that is below or underneath something.
  - **interpretation:** 零 (líng, "zero") sets a baseline or target level of nothingness. 下 (xià, "below") indicates a position or state that is beneath this baseline. Together, 零下 conveys the concept of measurements, typically temperature, that fall below zero, signifying negative values. The intuition is aiming below the absence of quantity, representing temperatures in the negative scale.
- **examples:**
  - 今( )天( )气(氣)温(溫)是( )零( )下( )五( )度( )。
    - Jīntiān qìwēn shì língxià wǔ dù.
    - Today's temperature is five degrees below zero.
  - 在( )零( )下( )的( )天( )气(氣)中( )，我( )们(們)需( )要( )穿( )厚( )外( )套( )。
    - Zài língxià de tiānqì zhōng, wǒmen xūyào chuān hòu wàitào.
    - In below zero weather, we need to wear thick coats.
  - 昨( )晚( )气(氣)温(溫)降( )到( )零( )下( )，让(讓)人( )觉(覺)得( )特( )别(別)冷( )。
    - Zuówǎn qìwēn jiàng dào língxià, ràng rén juédé tèbié lěng.
    - Last night the temperature dropped below zero, making it feel especially cold.
### 零下 → 零
- **definition:** zero; nil; fragment; fractional
- **pinyin:** líng
- **components:**
  - 雨
    - yǔ
    - rain
  - 令
    - lìng
    - command
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 雨 (yǔ, "rain") + 令 (lìng, "command") =
    - rain with large droplets as depicted in oracle script ->
    - associated with the loss or remainder of rain droplets ->
    - zero
  - **interpretation:** The character 零(líng) combines the semantic element of 雨 (yǔ, "rain") with the phonetic component 令 (lìng, "command"). Originally, it depicted raindrops falling from the sky, denoting something remaining or leftover. This visual representation of raindrops reduced to nothing contributed to its current meaning of "zero."
- **examples:**
  - 零( )是( )一( )种(種)数(數)字( )。
    - líng shì yī zhǒng shùzì.
    - Zero is a number.
  - 他( )的( )分( )数(數)是( )零( )。
    - tā de fēnshù shì líng.
    - His score is zero.
  - 他( )的( )希( )望( )几(幾)乎( )为(為)零( )，前( )途( )黯( )淡( )无(無)光( )。
    - tā de xīwàng jīhū wéi líng, qiántú àndàn wúguāng.
    - His hopes are nearly zero, and his future is bleak.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 零](@media/glyph96f6.png)
### 零下 → 零 → 雨
- **definition:** rain
- **pinyin:** yǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a cloud with drops of rain falling from it ->
    - horizontal stroke added later ->
    - rain
  - **interpretation:** 雨 (yǔ, "rain") visually represents rain falling from a cloud, capturing its essential form.
- **examples:**
  - 今天雨下得很大。
    - Jīntiān yǔ xià de hěn dà.
    - It rained hard today.
  - 他( )忘( )记(記)带(帶)伞(傘)，雨( )却(卻)毫( )不( )留( )情( )。
    - Tā wàngjì dài sǎn, yǔ què háobù liúqíng.
    - He forgot to bring an umbrella, and the rain showed no mercy.
  - 细(細)雨( )如( )丝(絲)，轻(輕)拂( )着(著)花( )瓣( )。
    - Xì yǔ rú sī, qīng fú zhe huā bàn.
    - The fine rain falls like silk, gently brushing the petals.

### 零下 → 零 → 令
- **definition:** command
- **pinyin:** lìng
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 卩
    - jié
    - seal
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 卩 (jié, "seal") =
    - person with seal ->
    - issuing orders or commands
  - **interpretation:** The character 令 (lǐng, "order") combines 人 (rén, "person") and 卩 (jié, "seal") to depict someone with a seal or authority, signifying the power to issue orders or commands.
- **examples:**
  - 将(將)军(軍)令( )部( )队(隊)保( )持( )警( )戒( )，士( )兵( )严(嚴)格( )服( )从(從)。
    - jiāngjūn lǐng bùduì bǎochí jǐngjiè, shìbīng yángé fúcóng.

  - 老( )师(師)令( )学(學)生( )认(認)真( )听(聽)讲(講)。
    - lǎoshī lǐng xuéshēng rènzhēn tīngjiǎng.
    - The teacher orders the students to listen attentively.
  - 国(國)王( )令( )大( )臣( )速( )速( )筹(籌)备(備)，迎( )接( )远(遠)方( )使( )节(節)。
    - guówáng lǐng dàchén sùsù chóubèi, yíngjiē yuǎnfāng shǐjié.
    - The king orders his ministers to quickly make preparations to welcome the foreign envoy.

### 零下 → 零 → 令 → 卩
- **definition:** seal
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那( )位( )卩( )正( )虔( )诚(誠)祈( )祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.

    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在( )庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式( )中( )，卩( )象( )征(徵)着(著)内(內)心( )的( )虔( )敬( )。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.

### 零下 → 下
- **definition:** below; under; next; to descend
- **pinyin:** xià
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - a line below another ->
    - later evolved into 下
  - **interpretation:** The character 下(xià, 'down') is an ideogram showing a line positioned below another line, visually representing 'below' or 'downward'. This layout intuitively depicts the concept of being beneath or beneath another object.
- **examples:**
  - 水( )从(從)山( )上( )流( )下( )。
    - Shuǐ cóng shān shàng liú xià.
    - The water flows down from the mountain.

## degree; measure word for temperature
### dù
---
- **definition:** degree; measure word for temperature
- **pinyin:** dù
- **components:**
  - 石
    - shí
    - rock
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 石 (shí, "rock") + 又 (yòu, "hand") =
    - hand measuring rock ->
    - 石 phonetic component for pronunciation ->
    - 石 corrupted to 𲟁
  - **interpretation:** The combination of a hand measuring a rock underlies the concept of measuring or gauging, leading to its meanings related to degree and limit. Over time, the rock component served as a phonetic element, though it was corrupted into another form.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )度( )过(過)了( )愉( )快( )的( )一( )天( )。
    - Tā dùguò le yúkuài de yītiān.
    - He spent a pleasant day.
  - 水( )的( )沸( )点(點)是( )100度( )。
    - Shuǐ de fèidiǎn shì yībǎi dù.
    - The boiling point of water is 100 degrees.
  - 这(這)次( )考( )试(試)的( )难(難)度( )很( )高( )。
    - Zhè cì kǎoshì de nándù hěn gāo.
    - This exam is very challenging.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 度](@media/glyph5ea6.png)
### 度 → 石
- **definition:** rock
- **pinyin:** shí
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stone beneath a cliff (厂) ->
    - distorted to 丆 ->
    - stone
  - **interpretation:** The character 石(shí, 'stone') originally depicted a stone under a cliff, representing the idea of a solid, natural object found at the base of rocky formations.
- **examples:**
  - 那( )个(個)花( )园(園)里(裡)有( )一( )块(塊)很( )大( )的( )石( )头(頭)。
    - Nàge huāyuán lǐ yǒu yīkuài hěn dà de shítou.
    - There is a big stone in the garden.
  - 石( )头(頭)变(變)得( )很( )滑( )，因( )为(為)下( )雨( )了( )。
    - Shítou biàn de hěn huá, yīnwèi xià yǔ le.
    - The stone became very slippery because it rained.
  - 他( )收( )集( )了( )很( )多( )不( )同( )种(種)类(類)的( )石( )头(頭)。
    - Tā shōujíle hěnduō bùtóng zhǒnglèi de shítou.
    - He collected many different kinds of stones.

### 度 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又( )」这(這)个(個)字( )最( )早( )来(來)源( )于(於)手( )。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很( )多( )汉(漢)字( )含( )有( )又( )部( )首( )，表( )示( )与(與)手( )有( )关(關)的( )动(動)作( )。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古( )人( )用( )又( )描( )绘(繪)手( )的( )形( )态(態)，体(體)现(現)了( )古( )汉(漢)字( )的( )独(獨)特( )魅( )力( )。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.

## 北方
---
## north; northern region
### běifāng
---
- **definition:** north; northern region
- **pinyin:** běifāng
- **components:**
  - 北
    - běi
    - north
  - 方
    - fāng
    - direction; region
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 北 (běi, "north") + 方 (fāng, "direction") =
    - the northern direction or region
  - **interpretation:** 北 (běi, "north") refers to the direction associated with the top of a traditional Chinese map, which is usually oriented with the south at the bottom. 方 (fāng, "direction") denotes a particular way or orientation. Combined, 北方 (běifāng) refers to the area or direction that is toward the north, thus it signifies both the north in terms of cardinal direction and the northern region geographically.
- **examples:**
  - 北方的冬天很冷。
    - Běifāng de dōngtiān hěn lěng.
    - The winter in the north is very cold.
  - 我( )计(計)划(劃)去( )北( )方( )旅( )行( )，看( )看( )那( )里(裡)的( )风(風)景( )。
    - Wǒ jìhuà qù běifāng lǚxíng, kàn kàn nàlǐ de fēngjǐng.
    - I plan to travel to the north and see the scenery there.
  - 北方人喜歡吃麵食。
    - Běifāng rén xǐhuān chī miànshí.
    - Northern people like to eat noodles.
### 北方 → 北
- **definition:** north
- **pinyin:** běi
- **components:**
  - 二
    - èr
    - two
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 背
    - bèi
    - back
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 二 (èr, "two") + 人 (rén, "person") =
    - two people back to back ->
    - originally meant "back"
  - **interpretation:** The character 北(běi) originally depicted two persons facing away from each other, signifying conflict or opposition, which metaphorically extended to refer to the direction "north" as something opposite. Over time, its meaning evolved, and its phonetic cousin 背(bèi, "back") took on the original sense directly associated with directionality and body position.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )住( )在( )北( )边(邊)。
    - Wǒ zhù zài běi biān.
    - I live in the north.
  - 北( )风(風)呼( )啸(嘯)，带(帶)走( )寒( )冷( )。
    - Běi fēng hūxiào, dài zǒu hán lěng.
    - The north wind howls, carrying away the cold.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 北](@media/glyph5317.png)
### 北方 → 北 → 二
- **definition:** two
- **pinyin:** èr
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts two parallel strokes ->
    - represents the number two
  - **interpretation:** The character 二 (èr, "two") consists of two horizontal lines that visually represent the concept of 'two'. This method of using parallel strokes to denote numbers is a straightforward representation of quantity, similar to how 一 (yī, "one") represents 'one' and 三 (sān, "three") represents 'three'.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )二( )支( )笔(筆)。
    - Wǒ yǒu èr zhī bǐ.
    - I have two pens.
  - 他( )买(買)了( )二( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )，我( )们(們)一( )起( )分( )享( )。
    - Tā mǎi le èr gè píngguǒ, wǒmen yīqǐ fēnxiǎng.
    - He bought two apples, and we shared them together.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 二](@media/glyph4e8c.png)

- **pinyin:** rén

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->

    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心( )灵(靈)获(獲)得( )了( )成( )长(長)。

### 北方 → 北 → 背
- **definition:** back
- **pinyin:** bèi
- **components:**
  - 北
    - běi
    - north
  - 月
    - yuè
    - meat
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 北 (běi, "north") + 月 (yuè, "meat") =
    - phonetic 北 + semantic 肉 (originally illustrated as 月) added to distinguish "back" from "north"
  - **interpretation:** The character 背(bèi, "back") was originally depicted by the character 北(běi, "north") alone because of their phonetic similarity. To explicitly convey the meaning related to the body, the semantic component 月(yuè, "meat"; originally styling 肉) was added, indicating the physical aspect of human anatomy.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )背( )着(著)书(書)包( )，去( )学(學)校( )。
    - Tā bèizhe shūbāo, qù xuéxiào.
    - He carries his schoolbag on his back and goes to school.
  - 他的背很直。
    - Tā de bèi hěn zhí.
    - His back is very straight.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 背](@media/glyph80cc.png)
### 北方 → 北 → 背 → 月
- **definition:** meat
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜( )空( )挂(掛)着(著)明( )月( )。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人( )们(們)赏(賞)月( )，寄( )托(託)相( )思( )。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 月](@media/glyph6708.png)
### 北方 → 方
- **definition:** direction; region
- **pinyin:** fāng
- **components:**
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - sword
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 一 (yī, "one") + 刀 (dāo, "sword") =
    - original depiction of blade's tip ->
    - borrowed for "side" ->
    - now "square"
  - **interpretation:** Initially depicting the blade of a sword, 方 (fāng, "square") was later borrowed for its current meaning due to its association with edges and boundaries, metaphorically expanded to define sides and squares.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)张(張)桌( )子( )是( )方( )的( )。
    - Zhè zhāng zhuōzi shì fāng de.
    - This table is square.
  - 院( )子( )里(裡)铺(鋪)满(滿)了( )方( )砖(磚)。
    - Yuànzi lǐ pū mǎn le fāng zhuān.
    - The courtyard is paved with square bricks.
  - 我( )买(買)的( )花( )瓶( )是( )方( )形( )的( )，设(設)计(計)简(簡)洁(潔)优(優)美( )。
    - Wǒ mǎi de huāpíng shì fāngxíng de, shèjì jiǎnjié yōuměi.
    - The vase I bought is square, with a simple and elegant design.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 方](@media/glyph65b9.png)
### 北方 → 方 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )一( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他( )只( )看( )到( )一( )只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了( )花( )园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.

    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.

## 春天
---
## spring
### chūntiān
---
- **definition:** spring
- **pinyin:** chūntiān
- **components:**
  - 春
    - chūn
    - spring
  - 天
    - tiān
    - sky; day
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 春 (chūn, "spring") refers to the season following winter, characterized by new growth and renewal. 天 (tiān, "sky; day") can mean the sky or represent the broader context of a day, often symbolizing an overarching period of time.
  - **interpretation:** 春 (chūn, "spring") is the season when nature revitalizes after winter, with a burst of life and growth. 天 (tiān, "day") relates to the overall span or time frame during which these transformations occur. Together, 春天 (chūntiān, "spring") encapsulates the notion of the spring season as a period marked by rejuvenation and renewal, governed by the conditions and influences of both earth and sky.
- **examples:**
  - 春( )天( )到( )来(來)时(時)，鸟(鳥)儿(兒)开(開)始( )歌( )唱( )。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, niǎoér kāishǐ gēchàng.
    - When spring arrives, the birds begin to sing.
  - 春( )天( )是( )个(個)美( )丽(麗)的( )季( )节(節)。
    - Chūntiān shì gè měilì de jìjié.
    - Spring is a beautiful season.
  - 在春天，花( )儿(兒)绽(綻)放( )出( )新( )芽( )。
    - Zài chūntiān, huāér zhànfàng chū xīnyá.
    - In spring, flowers bloom with new buds.
### 春天 → 春
- **definition:** spring
- **pinyin:** chūn
- **components:**
  - ⾠(艸)
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 屯
    - zhūn
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - ⾠(艸) (cǎo, "grass") + 日 (rì, "sun") + 屯 (zhūn, "sprout") =
    - sun shining on grass with sprouts ->
    - spring
  - **interpretation:** The character 春 (chūn, "spring") involves elements representing natural growth and revival: grass, sun, and sprouts together illustrate the vibrant growth occurring in springtime.
- **examples:**
  - 春( )天( )来(來)了( )。
    - Chūntiān láile.
    - Spring has arrived.
  - 春( )天( )来(來)了( )，万(萬)物( )复(復)苏(蘇)。
    - Chūntiān láile, wànwù fùsū.
    - Spring has arrived, and all things are reviving.
  - 春光明媚，人( )们(們)心( )情( )愉( )快( )。
    - Chūnguāng míngmèi, rénmen xīnqíng yúkuài.
    - The spring light is bright, and people feel joyful.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 春](@media/glyph6625.png)
### 春天 → 春 → ⾠
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a kind of agricultural tool used for tilling fields ->
    - original form of removing weeds ->
    - possibly related to tools or a person holding onto a cliff
  - **interpretation:** The character ⾠ initially represented a tool used for agricultural purposes, possibly related to removing weeds, symbolizing labor and cultivation. Alternatively, it is seen as depicting a person holding onto a cliff, illustrating support and elevation.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of ⾠](@media/glyph2fa0.png)
### 春天 → 春 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨( )曦( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日( )出( )东(東)方( )。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖( )的( )日( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)大( )地( )。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中( )午( )时(時)分( )，日( )高( )挂(掛)天( )。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 春天 → 春 → 屯
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** zhūn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a plant sprout (屮) with a middle emphasis line ->
    - emphasizes sprout
  - **interpretation:** The character 屯(tún, 'station') originally depicts a plant sprout with an added line to emphasize its growth. This imagery reflects the concept of development or establishment, leading to the sense of 'station' as a place where something is established or set up.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)附( )近( )有( )一( )个(個)储(儲)备(備)粮(糧)的( )屯( )。
    - Zhè fùjìn yǒu yīgè chǔbèi liáng de tún.
    - There is a grain storage station nearby.
  - 他( )们(們)准(準)备(備)在( )此( )地( )设(設)立( )一( )个(個)新( )的( )军(軍)事( )屯( )。
    - Tāmen zhǔnbèi zài cǐdì shèlì yīgè xīn de jūnshì tún.
    - They plan to establish a new military station at this location.
  - 村( )民( )们(們)在( )屯( )里(裡)储(儲)存( )了( )大( )量( )的( )粮(糧)食( )。
    - Cūnmín men zài tún lǐ chǔcún le dàliàng de liángshí.
    - The villagers have stored a large amount of grain in the station.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 屯](@media/glyph5c6f.png)
### 春天 → 天
- **definition:** sky; day
- **pinyin:** tiān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horizontal line above 大(dà, "big") to depict sky ->
    - anthropomorphic man with large head symbolizing heaven
  - **interpretation:** The character 天(tiān) originally depicts the sky as a horizontal line above a person with outstretched arms, 大(dà, "big"), emphasizing the vastness or domain of heaven. Over time, the character evolved into an anthropomorphic representation of heaven, which later influenced its interpretation in classical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 夜( )幕( )降( )临(臨)，天( )边(邊)星( )光( )闪(閃)烁(爍)。
    - Yèmù jiànglín, tiānbiān xīnguāng shǎnshuò.
    - As night falls, starlight gleams on the horizon.
  - 他仰望高空，祈( )求( )天( )佑( )众(眾)生( )。
    - Tā yǎngwàng gāokōng, qíqiú tiānyòu zhòngshēng.
    - He gazes up to the sky and prays for heaven's protection over all living beings.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 天](@media/glyph5929.png)

## 帮(幫)忙( )
---
## to help; to give assistance
### bāngmáng
---
- **traditional:** 幫忙
- **definition:** to help; to give assistance
- **pinyin:** bāngmáng
- **components:**
  - 幫
    - bāng
    - help; assist
  - 忙
    - máng
    - busy; hurry; be busy with
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 幫 (bāng, "help") + 忙 (máng, "busy") =
    - to help; to give assistance
  - **interpretation:** The word 幫忙 (bāngmáng, "to help; to give assistance") combines 幫 (bāng, "help") and 忙 (máng, "busy"). The term suggests the act of assisting someone who is busy, thus providing them with relief or support.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)你( )帮(幫)忙( )。
    - Qǐng nǐ bāngmáng.
    - Please help.
  - 我正在忙碌，无(無)法( )帮(幫)忙( )。
    - Wǒ zhèngzài mánglù, wúfǎ bāngmáng.
    - I am busy and cannot help.
  - 小( )明( )常( )常( )帮(幫)忙( )，他( )很( )受( )大( )家( )喜( )欢(歡)。
    - Xiǎomíng chángcháng bāngmáng, tā hěn shòu dàjiā xǐhuān.
    - Xiaoming often helps and is liked by everyone.
### 帮(幫)忙( ) → 幫
- **definition:** help; assist
- **pinyin:** bāng
- **components:**
  - 封
    - fēng
    - to seal
  - 帛
    - bó
    - silk
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 封 (phonetic) + 帛 (semantic, 'silk') ->
    - originally referring to the upper part of a shoe (鞋幫, 'shoe upper')
  - **interpretation:** The character 幫(bāng, "help") originally referred to the upper part of a shoe, indicating an early connection to crafting or constructing with fabric (silk). Over time, it extended to represent 'help' or 'assist,' possibly implying the act of supporting or holding together, analogous to how the upper shoe supports the foot.
  - **simplification:** 帮(幫): 干 (gān, 'dry') replaced 帛 (bó, 'silk') for phonetic simplification.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )帮(幫)你( )做( )作( )业(業)。
    - Wǒ bāng nǐ zuò zuòyè.
    - I help you do homework.
  - 老( )师(師)帮(幫)学(學)生( )解( )答( )问(問)题(題)。
    - Lǎoshī bāng xuéshēng jiědá wèntí.
    - The teacher helps the students answer questions.
  - 他( )会(會)帮(幫)朋( )友( )，解( )决(決)困( )难(難)。
    - Tā huì bāng péngyǒu, jiějué kùnnán.
    - He will help his friends solve difficulties.
### 帮(幫)忙( ) → 幫 → 封
- **definition:** to seal
- **pinyin:** fēng
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - dirt
  - 豐
    - fēng
    - seedling
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 土 (tǔ, "dirt") + phonetic 丰(豐) (fēng, "seedling") + semantic 寸 (cùn, "hand") ->
    - marking boundaries with seedlings ->
    - seal; close
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 丰(豐) (fēng, "seedling") as a phonetic element suggesting the sound, and 土 (tǔ, "dirt") and 寸 (cùn, "hand") as semantic elements. The combination symbolizes marking a boundary by planting seedlings in the ground, which is a way of sealing or enclosing an area. This concept naturally extends to sealing or closing something.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )亲(親)手( )封( )好( )信( )封( )。
    - Tā qīnshǒu fēng hǎo xìnfēng.
    - He personally sealed the envelope.
  - 我( )们(們)需( )要( )把( )窗( )户(戶)封( )住( )，以( )防( )寒( )风(風)进(進)入( )。
    - Wǒmen xūyào bǎ chuānghù fēng zhù, yǐ fáng hánfēng jìnrù.
    - We need to seal the windows to prevent the cold wind from entering.
  - 信( )件( )已( )经(經)被( )谨(謹)慎( )地( )密( )封( )。
    - Xìnjiàn yǐjīng bèi jǐnshèn de mìfēng.
    - The letter has been carefully sealed.
- **historical forms:**

    - abundance
  - **interpretation:** The character 豐(fēng, 'abundance') visually combines 𠁳, which depicts a pot overflowing with plants, and 豆(dòu, 'pot'), illustrating a vessel full of plenty. ### 帮(幫)忙( ) → 幫 → 封 → 豐 → 豆
- **definition:** pot
- **pinyin:** dòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a container ->
    - borrowed phonetically for the plant name
  - **interpretation:** The character 豆(dòu, 'drum') originally depicted a type of container. It was later borrowed for its phonetic value to represent the plant name 'bean', distinguishing it from a container. This transition indicates how the physical shape of the container, resembling a drum or storage pot, facilitated a phonetic borrowing.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )们(們)在( )课(課)堂( )上( )学(學)习(習)如( )何( )制(製)作( )豆( )。

    - Cūnzhuāng lǐ yǒu yí gè gǔlǎo de dòu, tā de shēngyīn hěn yǒu mèilì.

### 帮(幫)忙( ) → 幫 → 封 → 寸
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**

  - **interpretation:** The character combines 白 (bái, "white") for its phonetic value and 巾 (jīn, "cloth") for its semantic connection to textiles, resulting in the meaning of "silk," a type of cloth that often appears white.

### 帮(幫)忙( ) → 幫 → 帛 → 巾

### 帮(幫)忙( ) → 忙
- **definition:** busy; hurry; be busy with
- **pinyin:** máng
- **components:**
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - perish

    - heart in turmoil ->
    - busy
  - **interpretation:** 忙 (máng, "busy") combines 心 (xīn, "heart") for the emotional aspect with 亡 (wáng, "perish") which lends its sound, capturing the sense of a heart overwhelmed with activities.
- **examples:**

- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**

  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, "heart") originally depicted the shape of an actual heart, representing thoughts, emotions, and the core of a person. ## to help; to assist
### bāng
---
- **traditional:** 幫
- **definition:** to help; to assist
- **pinyin:** bāng
- **components:**
  - 巾
    - jīn
    - cloth
  - 邦
    - bāng
    - country
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 巾 (jīn, "cloth") + phonetic: 邦 (bāng, "country") =
    - assisting with cloth or materials ->
    - to help
  - **interpretation:** The character 幫 combines the meaning of 巾 (jīn, "cloth") with the phonetic element 邦 (bāng, "country"), symbolizing assistance or help with physical materials like cloth. This reflects the role of providing tangible support.
  - **simplification:** In the simplified form 帮, 巾 (jīn, "cloth") is retained while 邦 (bāng, "country") is kept intact from the traditional representation, aligning with historical simplification practices from 1956.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )来(來)帮(幫)你( )。
    - Wǒ lái bāng nǐ.
    - I will help you.
  - 他( )帮(幫)老( )师(師)，辅(輔)导(導)学(學)生( )。
    - Tā bāng lǎoshī, fǔdǎo xuésheng.
    - He helps the teacher, tutoring the students.
  - 遇( )到( )困( )难(難)时(時)，朋( )友( )会(會)帮(幫)忙( )。
    - Yùdào kùnnán shí, péngyǒu huì bāngmáng.
    - When encountering difficulties, friends will help.
### 帮(幫) → 巾
- **definition:** cloth
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a piece of cloth with two ends hanging down
  - **interpretation:** The character 巾(jīn, "cloth") visually represents a cloth or towel, with its depiction emphasizing the idea of a piece of fabric and its functionality.
- **examples:**
  - 爸( )爸( )用( )干(乾)净(淨)的( )巾( )擦( )手( )。
    - Bàba yòng gānjìng de jīn cā shǒu.
    - Dad uses a clean cloth to wipe his hands.
  - 她( )拿( )着(著)一( )条(條)巾( )，轻(輕)轻(輕)擦( )拭( )眼( )角( )。
    - Tā názhe yì tiáo jīn, qīngqīng cā shì yǎnjiǎo.
    - She holds a cloth and gently wipes the corners of her eyes.
  - 老( )人( )用( )巾( )给(給)手( )上( )包( )扎( )伤(傷)口( )。
    - Lǎorén yòng jīn gěi shǒu shàng bāozā shāngkǒu.
    - The elderly person uses a cloth to bandage the wound on his hand.

### 帮(幫) → 邦

  - 丰
    - fēng
    - abundant
  - 阝
    - fù
    - earthen mound

  - **type:** phono-semantic compound

    - Phonetic: 丰 (fēng, "abundant") + Semantic: 阝 (fù, "earthen mound") =
    - representation of an earthen mound + abundant resources ->
    - nation
  - **interpretation:** The character 邦(bāng, "nation") combines the idea of wealth or resources suggested by 丰 with the earthen boundary suggested by 阝, symbolizing a defined area with resources, which is the concept of a nation.
- **examples:**
  - 历(歷)史( )塑( )造( )了( )这(這)个(個)邦( )，使( )之( )繁( )荣(榮)昌( )盛( )。

- **definition:** abundant
- **pinyin:** fēng
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - ground
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a luxuriant plant growing on the ground (土) ->
    - modern version simplified, missing bottom stroke ->
    - similar to top component of 豐 (fēng, 'abundant') and 奉 (fèng, 'offer')
  - **interpretation:** The character 丰(豐) (fēng, 'abundant') originated as a pictogram depicting a plant thriving on the ground, symbolizing abundance. Over time, the detailed strokes representing the soil and growth were removed, simplifying the character.

## to stand
### zhàn
---
- **definition:** to stand
- **pinyin:** zhàn
- **components:**
  - 立
    - lì
    - stand
  - 占
    - zhān
    - divine; take possession of
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 立 (lì, "stand") + phonetic 占 (zhān) ->
    - to stand
  - **interpretation:** The character 站 represents the action of standing through the combination of 立 (lì, "stand"), which provides the semantic element of standing, and the phonetic 占 (zhān), which contributes the pronunciation. The semantic element 立 directly conveys the meaning of 'standing,' thus underscoring the character's overall meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )站( )在( )门(門)口( )。
    - Tā zhàn zài ménkǒu.
    - He is standing at the doorway.
  - 请(請)你( )站( )过(過)来(來)，我( )要( )给(給)你( )拍( )照( )。
    - Qǐng nǐ zhàn guòlái, wǒ yào gěi nǐ pāizhào.
    - Please stand over here, I want to take a photo of you.
  - 站久了，我就累了。
    - Zhàn jiǔle, wǒ jiù lèile.
    - After standing for a long time, I became tired.

### 站 → 占 → 口

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)

## 起

## to rise; to get up
### qǐ
---
- **definition:** to rise; to get up
- **pinyin:** qǐ
- **components:**
  - 走
    - zǒu
    - walk
  - 巳
    - sì
    - sixth of the Twelve Earthly Branches
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 走 (zǒu, "walk") + phonetic 巳 (sì) ->
    - rise; lift; begin; get up
  - **interpretation:** The semantic component 走 (zǒu, "walk") suggests movement or action, fitting with the meaning of rising or getting up. The phonetic component 巳 (sì) was chosen for its sound, contributing to the pronunciation without directly affecting the meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 太( )阳(陽)升( )起( )，天( )边(邊)染( )上( )橘( )色( )。
    - Tàiyáng shēng qǐ, tiānbiān rǎn shàng jú sè.
    - The sun rises, painting the sky with orange.
  - 我( )们(們)要( )起( )床( )了( )。
    - Wǒmen yào qǐchuáng le.
    - We need to get up.
  - 新( )的( )一( )天( )开(開)始( )了( )，大( )家( )都( )充( )满(滿)活( )力( )。
    - Xīn de yī tiān kāishǐ le, dàjiā dōu chōngmǎn huólì.
    - A new day begins, and everyone is full of energy.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 起](@media/glyph8d77.png)
### 起 → 走
- **definition:** walk
- **pinyin:** zǒu
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 夭
    - yāo
    - young
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
  - 龰
    - yuè
    - walking
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Running man (original depiction) + 止 (zhǐ, "foot") added later ->
    - top 夭 (yāo, "young") simplified to 土 (tǔ, "earth"), bottom stylized as 龰 ->
    - modern 走
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted a man running, with an added foot to emphasize movement. Over time, elements like the top 夭 were simplified to 土, and the bottom was stylized to 龰, although they are unrelated to the original meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 看( )到( )前( )方( )火( )光( )时(時)，他( )急( )忙( )走( )向( )安( )全( )地( )带(帶)。
    - Kàndào qiánfāng huǒguāng shí, tā jímáng zǒu xiàng ānquán dìdài.
    - When he saw the firelight ahead, he hurriedly ran toward safety.
  - 比( )赛(賽)开(開)始( )后(後)，选(選)手( )们(們)奋(奮)力( )走( )向( )终(終)点(點)。
    - Bǐsài kāishǐ hòu, xuǎnshǒu men fènlì zǒu xiàng zhōngdiǎn.
    - After the race began, the contestants ran towards the finish line.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 走](@media/glyph8d70.png)
### 起 → 走 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)的( )止( )需( )要( )静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他( )走( )路( )时(時)小( )心( )谨(謹)慎( )，因( )为(爲)止( )若( )受( )伤(傷)便( )难(難)前( )行( )。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

### 起 → 走 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )脚(腳)趾( )受( )伤(傷)了( )。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她( )用( )脚(腳)趾( )轻(輕)轻(輕)地( )踢( )了( )一( )下( )球( )。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在( )沙( )滩(灘)上( )散( )步( )时(時)，我( )感( )受( )到( )沙( )子( )在( )我( )的( )脚(腳)趾( )间(間)流( )动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 起 → 走 → 止 → 趾 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)后(後)，他( )的( )足( )不( )能( )动(動)。
    - tā shòushāng hòu, tā de zú bù néng dòng。
    - After he was injured, his foot couldn't move.
  - 小( )明( )打( )球( )时(時)，不( )小( )心( )扭( )伤(傷)了( )足( )。
    - xiǎo míng dǎ qiú shí, bù xiǎoxīn niǔ shāng le zú。
    - When Xiaoming was playing ball, he accidentally twisted his foot.
  - 我( )每( )天( )锻(鍛)炼(鍊)足( )部( )。

    - I exercise my foot muscles every day.

### 起 → 走 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 起 → 走 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )手( )写(寫)字( )。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我( )的( )手( )走( )路( )。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他( )的( )手( )很( )温(溫)暖( )，带(帶)给(給)我( )力( )量( )。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.

### 起 → 巳

  - **description:** Depicts a fetus or snake.
  - **interpretation:** The character 巳(sì, "fetus") likely represents the shape of a fetus curled in the womb or possibly the sinuous form of a snake. This ambiguity is due to its pictographic origin, imitating the curves and forms seen in nature.

    - The doctor found an abnormality in the fetus and urged the parents to pay early attention.

    - Mǔqīn gǎnshòudào sì wēiruò de xīntiào bànsuízhe wēnróu de xīwàng.

## 广(廣)州( )
---
## Guangzhou
### Guǎngzhōu
---
- **traditional:** 廣州
- **definition:** Guangzhou
- **pinyin:** Guǎngzhōu
- **components:**
  - 广(廣)
    - guǎng
    - broad; vast; wide
  - 州
    - zhōu
    - prefecture; administrative division; state; region
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 廣 (guǎng, "broad") refers to a vast area; 州 (zhōu, "prefecture") indicates a region or administrative division.
  - **interpretation:** 廣 (guǎng, "broad") highlights the geographic expansiveness or prominent status of the region. 州 (zhōu, "prefecture") reflects its historical and administrative significance as an important regional center. Together, 廣 (guǎng, "broad") + 州 (zhōu, "prefecture") denotes a large and significant administrative area, which is true for Guangzhou as a major city in southern China.
- **examples:**
  - 广(廣)州( )是( )一( )个(個)大( )城( )市( )。
    - Guǎngzhōu shì yī gè dà chéngshì.
    - Guangzhou is a big city.
  - 他( )们(們)计(計)划(劃)去( )广(廣)州( )旅( )游(遊)。
    - Tāmen jìhuà qù Guǎngzhōu lǚyóu.
    - They plan to travel to Guangzhou.
  - 广(廣)州( )拥(擁)有( )许(許)多( )美( )丽(麗)的( )景( )点(點)。
    - Guǎngzhōu yǒngyǒu xǔduō měilì de jǐngdiǎn.
    - Guangzhou has many beautiful attractions.
### 广(廣)州( ) → 广(廣)
- **traditional:** 廣
- **definition:** broad; vast; wide
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 廣
    - guǎng
    - broad
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广(廣) (guǎng, "broad") + phonetic 黃 (huáng, "yellow") ->
    - broad
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, "broad") combines the semantic element 广(廣), depicting a broad area or structure, with the phonetic element 黃 (huáng), which lends its sound. This combination signifies the idea of something wide or expansive.
  - **simplification:** 廣 was simplified to 广 by removing the 黃 (huáng, "yellow") phonetic component, leaving only the semantic element.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)条(條)河( )非( )常( )广(廣)阔(闊)。
    - Zhè tiáo hé fēicháng guǎngkuò.
    - This river is very broad.
  - 他( )的( )知( )识(識)面( )很( )广(廣)，总(總)是( )能( )解( )决(決)问(問)题(題)。
    - Tā de zhīshì miàn hěn guǎng, zǒng shì néng jiějué wèntí.
    - His knowledge is broad, and he is always able to solve problems.
  - 在( )学(學)校( )里(裡)，他( )参(參)加( )了( )许(許)多( )广(廣)泛( )的( )活( )动(動)。
    - Zài xuéxiào lǐ, tā cānjiāle xǔduō guǎngfàn de huódòng.
    - At school, he participated in many broad activities.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 广](@media/glyph5e7f.png)
### 广(廣)州( ) → 广(廣) → 廣
- **definition:** broad
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 广
    - guǎng
    - roof; shelter
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广 (roof; shelter) + phonetic 黃 (huáng, sound) ->
    - shelter
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, 'shelter') combines the semantic component 广, which suggests the idea of covering or enclosure like a roof, with the phonetic component 黃 (huáng). The enclosure aspect of 广 underlines the meaning of providing shelter or an expansive space.
  - **simplification:** 廣 was simplified to 广 by retaining the roof radical but removing 黃, simplifying the structure considerably.
- **examples:**
  - 我们正在寻找一个可以提供广(廣)的地方。
    - Wǒmen zhèngzài xúnzhǎo yī gè kěyǐ tígōng guǎng de dìfāng.
    - We are looking for a place that can provide shelter.
  - 那里的广(廣)设施非常完善，适合长时间停留。
    - Nàlǐ de guǎng shèshī fēicháng wánshàn, shìhé cháng shíjiān tíngliú.
    - The shelter facilities there are very complete, suitable for long stays.
  - 如果有恶劣天气，我们需要一个广(廣)来保护自己。
    - Rúguǒ yǒu èliè tiānqì, wǒmen xūyào yī gè guǎng lái bǎohù zìjǐ.
    - If there is bad weather, we need a shelter to protect ourselves.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 廣](@media/glyph5ee3.png)
### 广(廣)州( ) → 广(廣) → 廣 → 黃
- **definition:** yellow
- **pinyin:** huáng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally a pictogram depicting a disabled person or man with a ring of jade on the chest ->
    - phonetically borrowed for 'yellow' ->
    - 黃
  - **interpretation:** The character 黃 (huáng, 'yellow') originated from a pictogram representing either a disabled person or a man with a jade ring, showing a connection to cultural rituals or symbols of status. It was later phonetically borrowed to represent the color 'yellow' without semantic connection to its original depiction. In modern Chinese, its primary use is to denote the color yellow, disconnecting entirely from its debated pictographic origins.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)朵( )花( )是( )黄(黃)色( )的( )。
    - Zhè duǒ huā shì huángsè de.
    - This flower is yellow.
  - 秋( )天( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，树(樹)叶(葉)变(變)成( )金( )黄(黃)色( )。
    - Qiūtiān láilín shí, shùyè biàn chéng jīnhuáng sè.
    - When autumn arrives, the leaves turn golden yellow.
  - 他( )穿( )了( )一( )件( )黄(黃)色( )的( )外( )套( )。
    - Tā chuānle yī jiàn huángsè de wàitào.
    - He wore a yellow jacket.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 黃](@media/glyph9ec3.png)
### 广(廣)州( ) → 州
- **definition:** prefecture; administrative division; state; region
- **pinyin:** zhōu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an islet in a river
  - **interpretation:** 州 (zhōu, "administrative division") was originally a pictogram representing a small piece of land or islet amidst water, illustrating the ancient practice of using distinct land areas as administrative divisions.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )计(計)划(劃)参(參)观(觀)几(幾)个(個)州( )。
    - Wǒ jìhuà cānguān jǐ gè zhōu.
    - I plan to visit several states.
  - 美( )国(國)的( )各( )州( )都( )有( )独(獨)特( )的( )风(風)景( )。
    - Měiguó de gè zhōu dōu yǒu dútè de fēngjǐng.
    - Every state in the United States has unique scenery.
  - 州( )政( )府( )负(負)责(責)管( )理( )地( )方( )事( )务(務)，政( )策( )由( )州( )长(長)制( )定( )。
    - Zhōu zhèngfǔ fùzé guǎnlǐ dìfāng shìwù, zhèngcè yóu zhōu zhǎng zhìdìng.
    - The state government is responsible for managing local affairs, and the policies are set by the governor.
- **historical forms:**

### Guǎngzhōu

## Guangzhou

## 加
---
## to increase; to add
### jiā
---
- **definition:** to increase; to add
- **pinyin:** jiā
- **components:**
  - 力
    - lì
    - strength
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 力 (lì, "strength") + 口 (kǒu, "mouth") ->
    - exertion with additional effort or breath ->
    - add
  - **interpretation:** The character 加 (jiā, "add") combines 力 (lì, "strength"), indicating physical effort or force, with 口 (kǒu, "mouth"), suggesting either verbal command or the exertion of breath when effort is applied. This combination evokes the image of putting in more effort, hence the meaning "add" as in adding effort or increasing in quantity. The evolution from the effortful action to 'add' bridges the concept of augmenting or increasing.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)在( )茶( )里(裡)加( )些( )糖( )。
    - Qǐng zài chá lǐ jiā xiē táng.
    - Please add some sugar to the tea.
  - 你( )可( )以( )加( )我( )为(為)好( )友( )吗？
    - Nǐ kěyǐ jiā wǒ wéi hǎoyǒu ma?
    - Can you add me as a friend?
  - 我( )们(們)需( )要( )加( )倍( )努( )力( )，才( )能( )完( )成( )这(這)个(個)项(項)目( )。
    - Wǒmen xūyào jiābèi nǔlì, cái néng wánchéng zhège xiàngmù.
    - We need to double our efforts in order to complete this project.
- **historical forms:**

### 加 → 力
- **definition:** strength
- **pinyin:** lì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts either an arm bending out from the side of the body, or a wooden plough
  - **interpretation:** The character 力(lì, 'strength') visually represents physical power through the image of an arm or tool, emphasizing the fundamental concept of muscular force.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )尽(盡)全( )力( )，赢(贏)得( )比( )赛(賽)。
    - Tā yòng jìn quánlì, yíng dé bǐsài.
    - He used all his strength to win the competition.
  - 他( )把( )力( )气(氣)用( )在( )学(學)习(習)上( )。
    - Tā bǎ lìqì yòng zài xuéxí shàng.
    - He applies his strength to his studies.
  - 面( )对(對)困( )难(難)，他( )毫( )不( )退( )缩(縮)，全力以赴。
    - Miànduì kùnnán, tā háo bù tuìsuō, quánlì yǐ fù.
    - Facing difficulties, he neither retreats nor gives up, but goes all out.
- **historical forms:**

### 加 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

## 加

## 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報)
---
## weather forecast
### tiānqì yùbào
---
- **traditional:** 天氣預報
- **definition:** weather forecast
- **pinyin:** tiānqì yùbào
- **components:**
  - 天
    - tiān
    - sky; heaven
  - 气(氣)
    - qì
    - air; gas
  - 预(預)
    - yù
    - in advance; beforehand
  - 报(報)
    - bào
    - report; announce
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 天 (tiān, "sky; heaven") refers to the sky or the atmosphere. 氣 (qì, "air; gas") captures the concept of the air around us, often used in contexts related to the weather. 預 (yù, "in advance; beforehand") indicates something that is done ahead of time, pointing to the act of predicting or preparing. 報 (bào, "report; announce") involves conveying information, making it a natural fit for sharing predictions or announcements.
  - **interpretation:** The phrase combines 天 (tiān, "sky") and 氣 (qì, "air") to describe the 'state of the atmosphere,' essentially referring to 'weather.' 預 (yù, "in advance") and 報 (bào, "report") together signify 'reporting in advance,' which is the essence of forecasting as it informs people about future weather conditions. Thus, 天氣預報 (tiānqì yùbào) effectively means 'report on the condition of the sky and air expected in the future.'
- **examples:**
  - 今( )天( )的( )天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報)说(說)会(會)下( )雨( )。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì yùbào shuō huì xiàyǔ.
    - Today's weather forecast says it will rain.
  - 我( )们(們)应(應)该(該)常( )常( )查( )看( )天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報)，以( )便( )做( )好( )计(計)划(劃)。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi chángcháng chákàn tiānqì yùbào, yǐbiàn zuò hǎo jìhuà.
    - We should frequently check the weather forecast to make good plans.
  - 明( )天( )的( )天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報)很( )准(準)确(確)。
    - Míngtiān de tiānqì yùbào hěn zhǔnquè.
    - Tomorrow's weather forecast is very accurate.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 天
- **definition:** sky; heaven
- **pinyin:** tiān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horizontal line above 大(dà, "big") to depict sky ->
    - anthropomorphic man with large head symbolizing heaven
  - **interpretation:** The character 天(tiān) originally depicts the sky as a horizontal line above a person with outstretched arms, 大(dà, "big"), emphasizing the vastness or domain of heaven. Over time, the character evolved into an anthropomorphic representation of heaven, which later influenced its interpretation in classical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 夜( )幕( )降( )临(臨)，天( )边(邊)星( )光( )闪(閃)烁(爍)。
    - Yèmù jiànglín, tiānbiān xīnguāng shǎnshuò.
    - As night falls, starlight gleams on the horizon.
  - 他仰望高空，祈( )求( )天( )佑( )众(眾)生( )。
    - Tā yǎngwàng gāokōng, qíqiú tiānyòu zhòngshēng.
    - He gazes up to the sky and prays for heaven's protection over all living beings.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 天](@media/glyph5929.png)
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 气(氣)
- **traditional:** 氣
- **definition:** air; gas
- **pinyin:** qì
- **components:**
  - 米
    - mǐ
    - rice
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 氣 (phono-semantic: 气 for sound + 米 for meaning) ->
    - originally 'steam from cooked rice' ->
    - later 'air, flow'
  - **interpretation:** The character 氣 combines 气, representing the sound, with 米 (mǐ, 'rice'), suggesting the original meaning of steam emanating from cooked rice. Over time, the meaning shifted to encompass 'air' or 'flow', capturing the essence of movement or circulation.
  - **simplification:** 气(氣): 气 (qì, 'air') is a cursive shorthand of 氣, retaining the phonetic component but losing the semantic 米 ('rice').
- **examples:**
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)清( )晨( )的( )空( )气(氣)。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān qīngchén de kōngqì.
    - I like the morning air.
  - 呼( )吸( )新( )鲜(鮮)空( )气(氣)会(會)让(讓)人( )精( )神( )振( )奋(奮)。
    - Hūxī xīnxiān kōngqì huì ràng rén jīngshén zhènfèn.
    - Breathing fresh air invigorates the spirit.
  - 他( )对(對)我( )们(們)发(發)脾( )气(氣)，可( )能( )是( )因( )为(為)工( )作( )压(壓)力( )太( )大( )。
    - Tā duì wǒmen fā píqì, kěnéng shì yīnwèi gōngzuò yālì tài dà.
    - He got angry with us, possibly because his work pressure is too high.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 气](@media/glyph6c14.png)
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 气(氣) → 米
- **definition:** rice
- **pinyin:** mǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts rice kernels ->
    - 米(mǐ, 'rice')
  - **interpretation:** The character 米(mǐ, 'rice') visually represents dehusked rice kernels to differentiate it from 粟. The horizontal stroke may symbolize a bamboo sieve, emphasizing the process of separating grains from their husks.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)吃( )米( )饭(飯)。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī mǐfàn.
    - I like to eat rice.
  - 她( )从(從)农(農)村( )带(帶)回( )一( )袋( )米( )，用( )来(來)煮( )饭(飯)。
    - Tā cóng nóngcūn dài huí yī dài mǐ, yòng lái zhǔ fàn.
    - She brought a bag of rice from the countryside to cook.
  - 市( )场(場)上( )有( )新( )米( )出( )售( )。
    - Shìchǎng shàng yǒu xīn mǐ chūshòu.
    - New rice is available in the market.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 米](@media/glyph7c73.png)
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 预(預)
- **traditional:** 預
- **definition:** in advance; beforehand
- **pinyin:** yù
- **components:**
  - 頁
    - yè
    - page
  - 予
    - yǔ
    - to give
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 頁 (yè, "page") + phonetic 予 (yǔ) ->
    - anticipated response or preparation
  - **interpretation:** 頁 (yè, "page") suggests information or a plan, while 予 (yǔ) provides the sound, leading to the idea of preparation or arranging in advance. The concept of preparing or planning naturally precedes an event, reflecting the meaning 'in advance' or 'prepare'.
  - **simplification:** Simplified to 预 by reducing components 頁 to 页, retaining phonetic 予.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )提( )前( )通( )知( )了( )我( )们(們)，让(讓)我( )们(們)做( )好( )准(準)备(備)。
    - Tā tíqián tōngzhī le wǒmen, ràng wǒmen zuò hǎo zhǔnbèi.
    - He informed us in advance, letting us prepare well.
  - 他( )们(們)正( )在( )预(預)热(熱)机(機)器( )。
    - Tāmen zhèngzài yùrè jīqì.
    - They are preheating the machine.
  - 会(會)议(議)已( )经(經)预(預)定( )了( )时(時)间(間)和( )地( )点(點)。
    - Huìyì yǐjīng yùdìng le shíjiān hé dìdiǎn.
    - The meeting has already set the time and location beforehand.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 预(預) → 頁
- **definition:** page
- **pinyin:** yè
- **components:**
  - 首
    - shǒu
    - head; first
  - 卩
    - jié
    - kneeling person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 首 (head/face) + 卩 (kneeling person) ->
    - depicts a person's head and body
  - **interpretation:** Originally represented a head and its body in a kneeling posture, emphasizing “head”. The depiction was extended semantically to represent a 'page', as pages bear leading information like a head does for a body. The concept of 'head' is also reflected in its modern usage as a radical in characters related to parts of the head or face.
  - **simplification:** 页 is a cursive shorthand of the traditional 頁, simplifying the structure while maintaining the core shape of a head.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)打( )开(開)书(書)的( )第( )十( )页(頁)。
    - Qǐng dǎkāi shū de dì shí yè.
    - Please open to page ten of the book.
  - 这(這)本( )书(書)每( )一( )页(頁)都( )有( )插( )图(圖)。
    - Zhè běn shū měi yī yè dōu yǒu chātú.
    - Every page of this book has illustrations.
  - 我( )昨( )天( )晚( )上( )读(讀)了( )三( )十( )页(頁)。
    - Wǒ zuótiān wǎnshang dúle sānshí yè.
    - I read thirty pages last night.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 頁](@media/glyph9801.png)
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 预(預) → 頁 → 首
- **definition:** head; first
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of an animal with a long mouth and horns, often shown with or without hair ( 巛) ->
    - perpetuated as 𩠐 (form with hair) ->
    - streamlined to 首
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts the head of an animal, with prominent features like a long mouth and horns, emphasizing the notion of a 'head' both physically and symbolically as the foremost part.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )这(這)个(個)团(團)队(隊)的( )首( )领(領)。
    - Tā shì zhège tuánduì de shǒulǐng.
    - He is the head of this team.
  - 这(這)首( )歌( )是( )我( )最( )喜( )欢(歡)的( )歌( )曲( )。
    - Zhè shǒu gē shì wǒ zuì xǐhuān de gēqǔ.
    - This song is my favorite track.
  - 他( )抬( )起( )头(頭)，看( )向( )远(遠)方( )的( )山( )。
    - Tā tái qǐ tóu, kàn xiàng yuǎnfāng de shān.
    - He raised his head and looked towards the distant mountains.

### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 预(預) → 頁 → 卩
- **definition:** kneeling person
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那( )位( )卩( )正( )虔( )诚(誠)祈( )祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.
  - 礼(禮)仪(儀)师(師)指( )出( )，卩( )代( )表( )谦(謙)卑( )与(與)敬( )意( )。
    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在( )庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式( )中( )，卩( )象( )征(徵)着(著)内(內)心( )的( )虔( )敬( )。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.
- **historical forms:**
