### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 预(預) → 予
- **definition:** to give
- **pinyin:** yǔ
- **components:**
  - 呂
    - lǚ
    - spine
  - 亅
    - jué
    - hook
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** jiajie
  - **description:**
    - originally written as 呂 (lǚ, 'spine') phonetically borrowed ->
    - 亅 added for distinction and stylized ->
    - final form 予 (yǔ, 'give')
  - **interpretation:** The character 予(yǔ) ('give') is a borrowing for the meanings 'I; give', initially represented by 呂(lǚ) (‘spine’) due to phonetic similarity. A vertical stroke 亅 was later added at the bottom to differentiate it visually, resulting in a distinct character for the meaning 'to give'.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )愿(願)意( )予( )你( )帮(幫)助( )。
    - Wǒ yuànyì yǔ nǐ bāngzhù.
    - I am willing to give you help.
  - 这(這)项(項)荣(榮)誉(譽)被( )予( )了( )他( )。
    - Zhè xiàng róngyù bèi yǔ le tā.
    - This honor was given to him.
  - 她( )将(將)一( )份( )礼(禮)物( )予( )了( )我( )。
    - Tā jiāng yī fèn lǐwù yǔ le wǒ.
    - She gave a gift to me.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 予](@media/glyph4e88.png)
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 预(預) → 予 → 呂
- **definition:** spine
- **pinyin:** lǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts two disconnected blocks of metal, later connected in seal script ->
    - Original form of 鋁 (lǚ, 'ingot') ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'spine' and 'music notes'
  - **interpretation:** The character 呂(lǚ) ('two blocks of metal') visually represents two separate blocks aligned vertically. In its earliest forms, these blocks were disconnected, symbolizing distinct metal segments, which aligns with its early use for 'ingot'. Over time, as seen in seal script, a connecting line was added to form the modern appearance. This visual interpretation supports its original meaning related to metal. It was later phonetically borrowed to convey concepts like 'spine' and 'music notes', where no direct semantic link exists with metal, but the sound similarity allowed its reuse in these contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )两(兩)个(個)大( )的( )金( )属(屬)块(塊)铸(鑄)造( )了( )一( )个(個)雕( )像( )。
    - Tā yòng liǎng gè dà de jīnshǔ kuài zhùzào le yī gè diāoxiàng.
    - He cast a statue using two large blocks of metal.
  - 现(現)代( )工( )业(業)中( )，金( )属(屬)块(塊)常( )用( )于(於)制(製)造( )重( )型( )设(設)备(備)。
    - Xiàndài gōngyè zhōng, jīnshǔ kuài cháng yòng yú zhìzào zhòngxíng shèbèi.
    - In modern industry, metal blocks are often used for manufacturing heavy equipment.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)师(師)用( )金( )属(屬)块(塊)建( )造( )了( )一( )个(個)现(現)代( )化( )建( )筑(築)。
    - Zhège shèjì shī yòng jīnshǔ kuài jiànzào le yī gè xiàndàihuà jiànzhù.
    - The designer built a modern structure using metal blocks.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 呂](@media/glyph5442.png)
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 预(預) → 予 → 亅
- **definition:** hook
- **pinyin:** jué
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hook
  - **interpretation:** 亅 (jué, "hook") is a simple pictographic depiction of a hook, showing the elongated shape and the distinctive curve commonly associated with a hook.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)汉(漢)字( )的( )撇( )和( )亅( )总(總)是( )让(讓)我( )困( )惑( )。
    - Zhège hànzì de piě hé jué zǒng shì ràng wǒ kùnhuò.
    - The stroke and hook of this Chinese character always confuse me.
  - 她( )用( )钢(鋼)笔(筆)画(畫)了( )一( )个(個)带(帶)有( )亅( )的( )符( )号(號)。
    - Tā yòng gāngbǐ huà le yī gè dài yǒu jué de fúhào.
    - She drew a symbol with a hook using a pen.
  - 书(書)法( )作( )品( )中( )常( )能( )看( )到( )优(優)美( )的( )亅( )。
    - Shūfǎ zuòpǐn zhōng cháng néng kàn dào yōuměi de jué.
    - Elegant hooks are often seen in calligraphy works.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亅](@media/glyph4e85.png)
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 报(報)
- **traditional:** 報
- **definition:** report; announce
- **pinyin:** bào
- **components:**
  - 㚔
    - none
    - handcuffs
  - 𠬝
    - none
    - to subdue
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 㚔 (handcuffs) + 𠬝 (to subdue) =
    - to convict; to punish; to declare guilty
  - **interpretation:** The character 報 (bào, 'report; newspaper; recompense; respond') combines the imagery of handcuffs, symbolizing restraint, and an action of subduing, suggesting punishment or declaration of a verdict. This combination reflects the idea of delivering judgment or punishment, which extends metaphorically to mean 'reporting' or 'giving an account' of something. From delivering justice comes the idea of reciprocating actions, hence the sense of 'recompense' or 'respond'.
  - **simplification:** 报 is simplified from 報 by removing the 'handcuff' component 㚔, retaining the core representing the idea of reporting and responding without the punitive nuance.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )收( )到( )了( )一( )封( )信( )，里(裡)头(頭)有( )关(關)于(於)新( )项(項)目( )的( )详(詳)细(細)报(報)告( )。
    - Tā shōudào le yī fēng xìn, lǐtou yǒu guānyú xīn xiàngmù de xiángxì bàogào.
    - He received a letter with a detailed report about the new project.
  - 我( )每( )天( )都( )看( )早( )报(報)，了( )解( )世( )界( )发(發)生( )了( )什( )么(麼)。
    - Wǒ měitiān dū kàn zǎobào, liǎojiě shìjiè fāshēngle shénme.
    - I read the morning newspaper every day to understand what's happening in the world.
  - 他( )希( )望( )用( )自( )己( )的( )努( )力( )来(來)报(報)答( )父( )母( )的( )养(養)育( )之( )恩( )。
    - Tā xīwàng yòng zìjǐ de nǔlì lái bàodá fùmǔ de yǎngyù zhī ēn.
    - He hopes to use his own efforts to recompense his parents for their upbringing.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 报(報) → 㚔
- **definition:** handcuffs
- **pinyin:** none
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts handcuffs; originally a pictorial representation of shackles or restraints
  - **interpretation:** The character 㚔 is a pictogram that visually represents handcuffs. It does not rely on phonetic or semantic combinations with other components, instead directly depicting the shape and concept of handcuffs for its meaning. This iconography is consistent with its definition as a tool of restraint.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 㚔](@media/glyph3694.png)
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 报(報) → 𠬝
- **definition:** to subdue
- **pinyin:** none
- **components:**
  - 凡
    - fán
    - tray
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𠬝 (original pictogram for serving) ->
    - 凡 (fán, 'tray') added as semantic + 𠬝 (fú, 'to subdue') as phonetic ->
    - 服
  - **interpretation:** 𠬝 originally depicted the concept of serving or subduing. When 凡 (fán, 'tray') was added, it contributed to the meaning of serving or submitting, while 𠬝 provided the phonetic component. This later evolved into the character 服.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 𠬝](@media/glyph20b1d.png)
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 报(報) → 𠬝 → 凡
- **definition:** tray
- **pinyin:** fán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a plate or flat dish ->
    - borrowed for abstract meanings ->
    - unrelated to 几(幾) (jī, 'small table')
  - **interpretation:** 凡 (fán, 'ordinary') originally depicted a flat dish or plate. Over time, it expanded to encompass broader abstract meanings and is unrelated to the character 几(幾) which represents a small table.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )个(個)平( )凡( )的( )人( )。
    - tā shì gè píngfán de rén.
    - He is an ordinary person.
  - 凡( )人( )都( )可( )能( )犯( )错(錯)，从(從)错(錯)误(誤)中( )成( )长(長)。
    - fán rén dōu kěnéng fàncuò, cóng cuòwù zhōng chéngzhǎng.
    - Ordinary people may make mistakes, and grow from them.
  - 他凡去旅行，总(總)能( )发(發)现(現)新( )的( )风(風)景( )。
    - tā fán qù lǚxíng, zǒng néng fāxiàn xīn de fēngjǐng.
    - Whenever he travels, he always discovers new sceneries.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 凡](@media/glyph51e1.png)

## 晴天
---
## sunny day; clear sky
### qíngtiān
---
- **definition:** sunny day; clear sky
- **pinyin:** qíngtiān
- **components:**
  - 晴
    - qíng
    - clear; fine (weather)
  - 天
    - tiān
    - sky; day
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 晴 (qíng, "clear; fine (weather)") combines with 天 (tiān, "sky; day") to describe a day when the sky is clear and bright, free from clouds, resulting in a 'sunny day' or 'clear sky'.
  - **interpretation:** 晴 (qíng, "clear; fine (weather)") represents clarity and brightness in the weather, indicating no clouds or rain, which naturally results in 天 (tiān, "sky; day") presenting clear visibility. Therefore, 晴天 (qíngtiān) describes a day with a clear sky, usually under sunny conditions.
- **examples:**
  - 今天是晴天。
    - Jīntiān shì qíngtiān.
    - Today is a sunny day.
  - 我( )们(們)在( )晴( )天( )去( )公( )园(園)散( )步( )。
    - Wǒmen zài qíngtiān qù gōngyuán sànbù.
    - We go for a walk in the park on sunny days.
  - 晴( )天( )时(時)，我( )喜( )欢(歡)骑(騎)自( )行( )车(車)。
    - Qíngtiān shí, wǒ xǐhuān qí zìxíngchē.
    - I like to ride a bicycle on sunny days.
### 晴天 → 晴
- **definition:** clear; fine (weather)
- **pinyin:** qíng
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 青
    - qīng
    - green; blue
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 日 (rì, "sun") + phonetic 青 (qīng) ->
    - clear weather
  - **interpretation:** The sun 日 (rì, "sun") represents the element of daytime or light, and 青 (qīng) provides the phonetic sound. Together, they form 晴, indicating clear or fine weather, as sunlight naturally suggests clarity and brightness in the sky.
- **examples:**
  - 今( )天( )的( )天( )气(氣)很( )晴( )。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì hěn qíng.
    - Today's weather is very clear.
  - 早上的天空是晴的，真( )美( )丽(麗)。
    - Zǎoshang de tiānkōng shì qíng de, zhēn měilì.
    - The morning sky is clear, truly beautiful.
  - 雨( )后(後)总(總)是( )会(會)放( )晴( )。
    - Yǔ hòu zǒng shì huì fàng qíng.
    - It always clears up after the rain.
### 晴天 → 晴 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨( )曦( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日( )出( )东(東)方( )。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖( )的( )日( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)大( )地( )。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中( )午( )时(時)分( )，日( )高( )挂(掛)天( )。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 晴天 → 晴 → 青
- **definition:** green; blue
- **pinyin:** qīng
- **components:**
  - 生
    - shēng
    - life
  - 井
    - jǐng
    - well
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 生 (shēng, "life") + phonetic 井 (jǐng, "well") ->
    - final form
  - **interpretation:** The character 青(qīng, "green") originally combines the phonetic components 生(shēng, "life") and 井(jǐng, "well") for their sound values. The ancient interpretation associated 青(qīng) with the color of growing plants, possibly influenced by the idea of cinnabar for dyeing, reflecting a bluish-green shade common in nature. This phonetic pairing with 生 and 井 suggests a pronunciation that fits the word's meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 树(樹)叶(葉)是( )青( )色( )的( )。
    - Shùyè shì qīngsè de.
    - The leaves are green.
  - 青( )山( )环(環)绕(繞)着(著)村( )庄(莊)。
    - Qīngshān huánrào zhe cūnzhuāng.
    - Green hills surround the village.
  - 她( )有( )一( )双(雙)青( )色( )的( )眼( )睛( )。
    - Tā yǒu yī shuāng qīngsè de yǎnjīng.
    - She has a pair of green eyes.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 青](@media/glyph9752.png)
### 晴天 → 晴 → 青 → 生

- **pinyin:** shēng
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 屮 (chè, "sprout") on top of a horizontal line ->
    - signifies a plant sprouting from the ground ->
    - symbolizes life
  - **interpretation:** The character 生 (shēng, "life") represents the concept of life force or vitality, symbolized by a sprout emerging from the earth, embodying growth and renewal.
- **examples:**
  - 生( )命( )是( )一( )场(場)美( )丽(麗)的( )旅( )程( )。
    - Shēngmìng shì yī chǎng měilì de lǚchéng.
    - Life is a beautiful journey.
  - 他( )在( )战(戰)场(場)上( )奋(奮)力( )生( )存( )。
    - Tā zài zhànchǎng shàng fènlì shēngcún.
    - He fights to live on the battlefield.
  - 这(這)家( )餐( )厅(廳)的( )生( )鱼(魚)片( )非( )常( )新( )鲜(鮮)。
    - Zhè jiā cāntīng de shēngyúpiàn fēicháng xīnxiān.
    - The raw fish slices at this restaurant are very fresh.

### 晴天 → 晴 → 青 → 生 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春( )雨( )滋( )润(潤)后(後)，小( )屮( )冲(沖)破( )泥( )土( )而( )出( )。

### 晴天 → 晴 → 青 → 井
- **definition:** well
- **pinyin:** jǐng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a grid symbolizing a well's structure
  - **interpretation:** The character 井 (jǐng, "well") visually represents the framework or grid of wooden or stone beams that would make up the top view of a traditional well, highlighting its function and design.
- **examples:**
  - 村口有一口老井。
    - Cūnkǒu yǒuyī kǒu lǎo jǐng.
    - There is an old well at the village entrance.

    - Xiàtiān kùrè shí, jǐng shuǐ dàilái zhèn zhèn liángyì.

### 晴天 → 天
- **definition:** sky; day
- **pinyin:** tiān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horizontal line above 大(dà, "big") to depict sky ->
    - anthropomorphic man with large head symbolizing heaven
  - **interpretation:** The character 天(tiān) originally depicts the sky as a horizontal line above a person with outstretched arms, 大(dà, "big"), emphasizing the vastness or domain of heaven. Over time, the character evolved into an anthropomorphic representation of heaven, which later influenced its interpretation in classical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 夜( )幕( )降( )临(臨)，天( )边(邊)星( )光( )闪(閃)烁(爍)。
    - Yèmù jiànglín, tiānbiān xīnguāng shǎnshuò.
    - As night falls, starlight gleams on the horizon.
  - 他仰望高空，祈( )求( )天( )佑( )众(眾)生( )。
    - Tā yǎngwàng gāokōng, qíqiú tiānyòu zhòngshēng.
    - He gazes up to the sky and prays for heaven's protection over all living beings.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 天](@media/glyph5929.png)

## 中( )国(國)民( )航( )
---
## Civil Aviation Administration of China (CAAC)
### Zhōngguó Mínháng
---
- **traditional:** 中國民航
- **definition:** Civil Aviation Administration of China (CAAC)
- **pinyin:** Zhōngguó Mínháng
- **components:**
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
  - 國
    - guó
    - country
  - 民
    - mín
    - people; citizen
  - 航
    - háng
    - navigation; sailing; flight
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 中 (zhōng, "middle") + 國 (guó, "country") =
    - 中國 (Zhōngguó, "China"); 民 (mín, "people") shares a semantic connection with "citizenship"; 航 (háng, "navigation") suggests the act of navigating or flying.
  - **interpretation:** 中國 (Zhōngguó, "China") represents the country; 民 (mín, "people") implies the national citizenry involved in aviation processes; 航 (háng, "navigation") focuses on flight and air travel. Together, 中國民航 (Zhōngguó Mínháng) denotes China's organized air operations involving citizens — thus representing the Civil Aviation Administration of China.
- **examples:**
  - 中( )国(國)民( )航( )是一个重要的机构。
    - Zhōngguó Mínháng shì yīgè zhòngyào de jīgòu.
    - The Civil Aviation Administration of China is an important organization.
  - 中( )国(國)民( )航( )的航班准点率很高。
    - Zhōngguó Mínháng de hángbān zhǔndiǎn lǜ hěn gāo.
    - The punctuality rate of flights by the Civil Aviation Administration of China is very high.
  - 很( )多( )人( )关(關)注( )中( )国(國)民( )航( )的最新政策。
    - Hěn duō rén guānzhù Zhōngguó Mínháng de zuìxīn zhèngcè.
    - Many people are paying attention to the latest policies of the Civil Aviation Administration of China.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 中
- **definition:** middle
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看( )着(著)远(遠)方( )。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房( )间(間)正( )中( )，挂(掛)着(著)一( )幅( )名( )画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.

### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 國
- **definition:** country
- **pinyin:** guó
- **components:**
  - 囗
    - wéi
    - closure
  - 或
    - huò
    - or
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 囗 (wéi, "closure") + phonetic 或 (huò, "or") ->
    - enclosed area signifying a state or country
  - **interpretation:** The character 國 (guó, "country") combines the idea of an enclosed space from 囗 (wéi, "closure") with the phonetic component 或 (huò, "or"), suggesting a defined and protected area, aligning with the concept of a country or state.
  - **simplification:** The simplified character 国(國) uses 玉 (yù, "jade") as a mnemonic for wealth within an enclosure, dropping the component 或 (huò, "or") for simplicity.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)国(國)有( )着(著)独(獨)特( )魅( )力( )。
    - Zhège guó yǒuzhe dútè mèilì.
    - This country has a unique charm.
  - 许(許)多( )人( )热(熱)爱(愛)国(國)文( )化( )，努( )力( )建( )设(設)国(國)的( )美( )好( )明( )天( )。
    - Xǔduō rén rè'ài guó wénhuà, nǔlì jiànshè guó de měihǎo míngtiān.
    - Many people cherish their country's culture and strive to build a better future.

### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 國 → 或 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。

    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.

### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 國 → 或 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )一( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )。

    - I have one apple.

    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一( )条(條)直( )路( )通( )向( )远(遠)方( )。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.

### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 民

- **pinyin:** mín
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts an eye stabbed by a needle, symbolizing oppression of the people ->
    - people
  - **interpretation:** The character 民 (mín, 'people') originally depicted an eye being pierced by a tool, a metaphor for the suffering and experiences of the common people. This imagery evolved to represent the broader concept of the populace.
- **examples:**

### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 航 → 亢 → 亠
- **definition:** symbol for high position
- **pinyin:** tóu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Couvercle with a handle ->
    - false friend: roof of a tower in 高 (gāo, "high") ->
    - head and open arms in 立 (lì, "stand")/交 (jiāo, "exchange") ->
    - roof of a hut in 六 (liù, "six") ->
    - top of traditional cloth in 衣 (yī, "clothing") ->
    - mark over silk threads in 玄 (xuán, "mysterious") ->
    - top of knife/chisel to mark prisoners in 辛 (xīn, "bitter") ->
    - grass in 离 (lí, "leave")
  - **interpretation:** 亠 is primarily a pictogram that initially represented a cover with a handle. However, its usage varies in different characters, symbolizing roofs, heads, tops of clothing, and marks, showing its flexibility and evolution in form and meaning across contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 在( )汉(漢)字( )结(結)构(構)中( )，亠( )作( )为(為)顶(頂)标(標)发(發)挥(揮)作( )用( )。
    - Zài hànzì jiégòu zhōng, tóu zuòwéi dǐngbiāo fāhuī zuòyòng.
    - In the structure of Chinese characters, 亠 acts as a top mark to exert its function.
  - 古( )代( )书(書)法( )作( )品( )中( )，亠( )显(顯)示( )出( )独(獨)特( )的( )审(審)美( )价(價)值( )。
    - Gǔdài shūfǎ zuòpǐn zhōng, tóu xiǎnshì chū dútè de shěnměi jiàzhí.
    - In ancient calligraphy, 亠 demonstrates a unique aesthetic value.

## 起( )飞(飛)
---
## to take off
### qǐfēi
---
- **traditional:** 起飛
- **definition:** to take off
- **pinyin:** qǐfēi
- **components:**
  - 起
    - qǐ
    - rise; initiate; begin; get up
  - 飛
    - fēi
    - fly; flutter; hover; rush
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 起 (qǐ, "rise") + 飛 (fēi, "fly") =
    - rise up to fly ->
    - take off
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 起 (qǐ, "rise") and 飛 (fēi, "fly") conveys the action of an aircraft lifting off the ground to begin flying. This is a straightforward and literal representation of the concept of taking off.
- **examples:**
  - 飞(飛)机(機)起( )飞(飛)。
    - Fēijī qǐfēi.
    - The airplane takes off.
  - 飞(飛)机(機)在( )跑( )道( )上( )加( )速( )，很( )快( )起( )飞(飛)。
    - Fēijī zài pǎodào shàng jiāsù, hěn kuài qǐfēi.
    - The airplane accelerates on the runway, then takes off quickly.
  - 准(準)备(備)完( )毕(畢)，飞(飛)机(機)起( )飞(飛)。
    - Zhǔnbèi wánbì, fēijī qǐfēi.
    - After getting ready, the airplane takes off.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起
- **definition:** rise; initiate; begin; get up
- **pinyin:** qǐ
- **components:**
  - 走
    - zǒu
    - walk
  - 巳
    - sì
    - sixth of the Twelve Earthly Branches
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 走 (zǒu, "walk") + phonetic 巳 (sì) ->
    - rise; lift; begin; get up
  - **interpretation:** The semantic component 走 (zǒu, "walk") suggests movement or action, fitting with the meaning of rising or getting up. The phonetic component 巳 (sì) was chosen for its sound, contributing to the pronunciation without directly affecting the meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 太( )阳(陽)升( )起( )，天( )边(邊)染( )上( )橘( )色( )。
    - Tàiyáng shēng qǐ, tiānbiān rǎn shàng jú sè.
    - The sun rises, painting the sky with orange.
  - 我( )们(們)要( )起( )床( )了( )。
    - Wǒmen yào qǐchuáng le.
    - We need to get up.
  - 新( )的( )一( )天( )开(開)始( )了( )，大( )家( )都( )充( )满(滿)活( )力( )。
    - Xīn de yī tiān kāishǐ le, dàjiā dōu chōngmǎn huólì.
    - A new day begins, and everyone is full of energy.

### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走
- **definition:** walk
- **pinyin:** zǒu
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 夭
    - yāo
    - young
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
  - 龰
    - yuè
    - walking
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Running man (original depiction) + 止 (zhǐ, "foot") added later ->
    - top 夭 (yāo, "young") simplified to 土 (tǔ, "earth"), bottom stylized as 龰 ->
    - modern 走
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted a man running, with an added foot to emphasize movement. Over time, elements like the top 夭 were simplified to 土, and the bottom was stylized to 龰, although they are unrelated to the original meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 看( )到( )前( )方( )火( )光( )时(時)，他( )急( )忙( )走( )向( )安( )全( )地( )带(帶)。
    - Kàndào qiánfāng huǒguāng shí, tā jímáng zǒu xiàng ānquán dìdài.
    - When he saw the firelight ahead, he hurriedly ran toward safety.
  - 比( )赛(賽)开(開)始( )后(後)，选(選)手( )们(們)奋(奮)力( )走( )向( )终(終)点(點)。
    - Bǐsài kāishǐ hòu, xuǎnshǒu men fènlì zǒu xiàng zhōngdiǎn.
    - After the race began, the contestants ran towards the finish line.

### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 止

- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)的( )止( )需( )要( )静(靜)养(養)。

    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.

### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )脚(腳)趾( )受( )伤(傷)了( )。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她( )用( )脚(腳)趾( )轻(輕)轻(輕)地( )踢( )了( )一( )下( )球( )。

    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在( )沙( )滩(灘)上( )散( )步( )时(時)，我( )感( )受( )到( )沙( )子( )在( )我( )的( )脚(腳)趾( )间(間)流( )动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 止 → 趾 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)后(後)，他( )的( )足( )不( )能( )动(動)。
    - tā shòushāng hòu, tā de zú bù néng dòng。
    - After he was injured, his foot couldn't move.
  - 小( )明( )打( )球( )时(時)，不( )小( )心( )扭( )伤(傷)了( )足( )。

  - 我( )每( )天( )锻(鍛)炼(鍊)足( )部( )。

### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )手( )写(寫)字( )。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我( )的( )手( )走( )路( )。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他( )的( )手( )很( )温(溫)暖( )，带(帶)给(給)我( )力( )量( )。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.

### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 土

- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民( )耕( )土( )，种(種)出( )丰(豐)收( )。

### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 巳
- **definition:** sixth of the Twelve Earthly Branches
- **pinyin:** sì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a fetus or snake.
  - **interpretation:** The character 巳(sì, "fetus") likely represents the shape of a fetus curled in the womb or possibly the sinuous form of a snake. This ambiguity is due to its pictographic origin, imitating the curves and forms seen in nature.
- **examples:**
  - 那小小的巳在( )温(溫)暖( )的( )子( )宫(宮)中( )悄( )然( )成( )长(長)。
    - Nà xiǎoxiǎo de sì zài wēnnuǎn de zǐgōng zhōng qiǎorán chéngzhǎng.
    - The tiny fetus is growing quietly in the warm womb.
  - 医(醫)生( )发(發)现(現)巳( )异(異)常( )，提( )醒( )家( )长(長)早( )期( )注( )意( )。
    - Yīshēng fāxiàn sì yìcháng, tíxǐng jiāzhǎng zǎoqī zhùyì.
    - The doctor found an abnormality in the fetus and urged the parents to pay early attention.
  - 母( )亲(親)感( )受( )到( )巳( )微( )弱( )的( )心( )跳( )伴( )随(隨)着(著)温(溫)柔( )的( )希( )望( )。
    - Mǔqīn gǎnshòudào sì wēiruò de xīntiào bànsuízhe wēnróu de xīwàng.
    - The mother felt the fetus's faint heartbeat accompanied by a gentle hope.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 巳](@media/glyph5df3.png)
### 起( )飞(飛) → 飛
- **definition:** fly; flutter; hover; rush
- **pinyin:** fēi
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bird flying upwards
  - **interpretation:** The character 飛(fēi, "fly") depicts the image of a bird in flight, which naturally evokes the concepts of flying, fluttering, or hovering as a bird does in the sky.
  - **simplification:** 飞 is a simplified form of 飛, created by reducing the complexity of the character while maintaining its original flying bird form.
- **examples:**
  - 小( )鸟(鳥)在( )空( )中( )飞(飛)翔( )。
    - Xiǎo niǎo zài kōngzhōng fēixiáng.
    - The bird is flying in the sky.
  - 秋( )天( )来(來)了( )，树(樹)叶(葉)纷(紛)纷(紛)飞(飛)落( )。
    - Qiūtiān láile, shùyè fēnfēn fēiluò.
    - Autumn has arrived, and leaves are fluttering down.
  - 时(時)间(間)飞(飛)快( )地( )流( )逝( )。
    - Shíjiān fēikuài de liúshì.
    - Time flies by quickly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 飛](@media/glyph98db.png)

## 停( )车(車)场(場)
---
## parking lot
### tíngchēchǎng
---
- **traditional:** 停車場
- **definition:** parking lot
- **pinyin:** tíngchēchǎng
- **components:**
  - 停
    - tíng
    - stop; halt
  - 車
    - chē
    - vehicle; car
  - 場
    - chǎng
    - field; place; venue
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 停 (tíng, "stop"), 車 (chē, "vehicle"), 場 (chǎng, "field; place")
  - **interpretation:** The word 停車場 (tíngchēchǎng) combines 停 (tíng, "stop"), 車 (chē, "vehicle"), and 場 (chǎng, "field; place") to refer to a designated area where vehicles are stopped and parked. This combination makes sense because it specifies a place specifically meant for the cessation and storage of vehicles.
- **examples:**
  - 停( )车(車)场(場)很( )大( )。
    - Tíngchēchǎng hěn dà.
    - The parking lot is very large.
  - 我( )去( )停( )车(車)场(場)，寻(尋)找( )一( )个(個)空( )位( )。
    - Wǒ qù tíngchēchǎng, xúnzhǎo yīgè kòngwèi.
    - I go to the parking lot to look for an empty spot.
  - 早( )晨( )上( )班( )时(時)，停( )车(車)场(場)已( )经(經)满(滿)了( )。
    - Zǎochén shàngbān shí, tíngchēchǎng yǐjīng mǎnle.
    - During the morning rush, the parking lot is already full.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停
- **definition:** stop; halt
- **pinyin:** tíng
- **components:**
  - 亻
    - rén
    - person
  - 亭
    - tíng
    - pavilion
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Semantic 亻 (rén, "person") + Phonetic 亭 (tíng, "pavilion") ->
    - associated with a place where people stop or rest ->
    - "to stop; to park"
  - **interpretation:** The character 停(tíng) combines the person radical 亻 to show that stopping is an action related to humans, with the phonetic component 亭 to provide pronunciation. The meaning evolves from a person staying or pausing, similar to resting in a pavilion.
- **examples:**
  - 车(車)子( )停( )在( )路( )旁( )边(邊)。
    - Chēzǐ tíng zài lù pángbiān.
    - The car stopped by the roadside.
  - 司( )机(機)停( )车(車)时(時)，调(調)整( )方( )向( )后(後)再( )出( )发(發)。
    - Sījī tíngchē shí, tiáozhěng fāngxiàng hòu zài chūfā.
    - The driver, after parking, adjusted the steering before setting off again.
  - 因( )为(為)大( )雪( )，学(學)校( )停( )课(課)。
    - Yīnwèi dàxuě, xuéxiào tíngkè.
    - Due to heavy snow, school classes were canceled.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 停](@media/glyph505c.png)
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停 → 亻
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Stylization of 人 (rén, "person") as a side radical to depict a person
  - **interpretation:** 亻 is a stylized form of 人 (rén, "person") used to indicate human-related meanings when combined with other components in characters as a radical. It visually represents a standing person, maintaining the core meaning of 'person' while facilitating the construction of complex characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )一( )个(個)热(熱)心( )的( )人( )。
    - Tā shì yī gè rèxīn de rén.
    - He is a kind-hearted person.
  - 这(這)座( )城( )市( )里(裡)住( )着(著)很( )多( )优(優)秀( )的( )人( )。
    - Zhè zuò chéngshì lǐ zhùzhe hěn duō yōuxiù de rén.
    - There are many outstanding people living in this city.
  - 每( )个(個)人( )都( )有( )梦(夢)想( )。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu mèngxiǎng.
    - Everyone has dreams.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停 → 亻 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )个(個)好( )人( )。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每( )个(個)人( )都( )有( )责(責)任( )，为(為)社( )会(會)作( )出( )贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心( )灵(靈)获(獲)得( )了( )成( )长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.

### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停 → 亭
- **definition:** pavilion
- **pinyin:** tíng
- **components:**
  - 京
    - jīng
    - capital
  - 丁
    - dīng
    - nail
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:** semantic 京 (jīng, 'capital') variant, stylized as tower + phonetic 丁 (dīng, 'nail')
  - **interpretation:** The character 亭(tíng, 'pavilion') combines a variant of 京 (jīng, 'capital city'), stylized to resemble a tower or platform, with 丁 (dīng, 'nail') as the phonetic component. This representation suggests a small, fixed structure such as a pavilion, where the 'tower-like' form conveys the sense of an elevated, ornamental building.
- **examples:**
  - 在( )公( )园(園)里(裡)有( )一( )个(個)漂( )亮( )的( )亭( )子( )。

    - There is a beautiful pavilion in the park.
  - 我( )们(們)坐( )在( )亭( )里(裡)，欣( )赏(賞)周( )围(圍)的( )风(風)景( )。
    - Wǒmen zuò zài tíng lǐ, xīnshǎng zhōuwéi de fēngjǐng.
    - We sit in the pavilion, enjoying the surrounding scenery.
  - 亭( )子( )的( )屋( )顶(頂)是( )用( )传(傳)统(統)的( )瓦( )片( )做( )的( )。
    - Tíngzi de wūdǐng shì yòng chuántǒng de wǎpiàn zuò de.
    - The roof of the pavilion is made with traditional tiles.

### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停 → 亭 → 京
- **definition:** capital
- **pinyin:** jīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tall building or tower
  - **interpretation:** The character 京 (jīng, "tower") is a pictogram representing a tall building or a tower. Its form directly illustrates the concept of height and grandeur associated with a prominent structure.
- **examples:**
  - 故( )宫(宮)的( )塔( )楼(樓)很( )高( )。
    - Gùgōng de tǎlóu hěn gāo.

    - Zài Běijīng, nǐ kěyǐ kàn dào xǔduō gāolóu dàshà.
    - In Beijing, you can see many tall buildings.

    - Gǔdài de jiànzhú zhōng chángcháng néng jiàn dào gāosǒng de tǎdǐng.

### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停 → 亭 → 丁
- **definition:** nail
- **pinyin:** dīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of a nail ->
    - 丁
  - **interpretation:** The character 丁 originally depicted the head of a nail, emphasizing simplicity and directness. While it has developed other interpretations over time, such as a head or city wall, these relate to similar shapes and functions. Today, 釘 (dīng, 'nail') reflects this meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 工( )人( )熟( )练(練)地( )把( )丁( )敲( )进(進)了( )墙(牆)壁( )。

    - The worker skillfully hammered the nail into the wall.
  - 他( )精( )心( )挑( )选(選)了( )铁(鐵)质(質)丁( )，确(確)保( )家(傢)具(俱)稳(穩)固( )。
    - Tā jīngxīn tiāoxuǎnle tiě zhì dīng, quèbǎo jiājù wěngù.
    - He carefully selected the iron nail to ensure the furniture was stable.
  - 请(請)把( )散( )落( )的( )丁( )收( )好( )。
    - Qǐng bǎ sànluò de dīng shōuhǎo.
    - Please gather the scattered nails.

### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 車
- **definition:** vehicle; car
- **pinyin:** chē
- **components:**
  - 田
    - tián
    - field
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a carriage viewed from above; wheels on both sides + sun shade on top ->
    - depicted vertically with wheels as strokes and loading area marked by 田 (tián, "field") ->
    - 車
  - **interpretation:** The character 車(chē, "vehicle") originally depicts a carriage from an overhead perspective. The transformation into the vertical form involved simplifying the depiction of wheels and emphasizing the loading area, marked by a field symbol, creating a streamlined pictographic representation.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 車 was simplified to 车 by reducing the number of strokes, maintaining the overall shape of the vehicle but removing intricate details.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )坐( )车(車)去( )上( )班( )。
    - Wǒ zuò chē qù shàngbān.
    - I take a car to go to work.
  - 这(這)辆(輛)车(車)很( )快( )。
    - Zhè liàng chē hěn kuài.
    - This car is very fast.
  - 我( )想( )买(買)一( )辆(輛)新( )车(車)。
    - Wǒ xiǎng mǎi yī liàng xīn chē.
    - I want to buy a new car.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 車](@media/glyph8eca.png)

### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場
- **definition:** field; place; venue
- **pinyin:** chǎng
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
  - 昜
    - yáng
    - sun rising

  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 土 (tǔ, "earth") + phonetic 昜 (yáng) ->
    - open area on earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 場 (chǎng, "field; place; venue") pairs 土 (tǔ, "earth") suggesting a physical space or ground, with 昜 (yáng) as the phonetic component. This combination conveys the idea of an open area that is associated with land or ground, leading to the meaning of a 'field' or 'place'.
- **examples:**

    - After the movie started, everyone was very quiet.
  - 他( )在( )足( )球( )场(場)上( )踢( )得( )很( )好( )。
    - Tā zài zúqiú chǎng shàng tī de hěn hǎo.
    - He plays very well on the soccer field.

- **pinyin:** tǔ

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth

### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場 → 昜

- **pinyin:** yáng
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì

  - 丂

  - **description:**

    - rays of the sun shining over a tree branch
  - **interpretation:** The character 昜(yáng) portrays the concept of the sun's rays shining down, symbolized by 日 (rì, "sun") with 丂 representing a tree branch and 彡 depicting the sun's rays. This compound visually encapsulates the light given off by the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 日( )光( )照( )耀( )下( )时(時)，旗( )帜(幟)高( )昜( )飘(飄)扬(揚)。

    - Fēng ér chuīguò liǔ shāo shí, xīn zhōng de mèngxiǎng yě suí yáng qǐ.
    - As the wind passes the tips of the willows, the dreams in the heart rise as well.

### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場 → 昜 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨( )曦( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日( )出( )东(東)方( )。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖( )的( )日( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)大( )地( )。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中( )午( )时(時)分( )，日( )高( )挂(掛)天( )。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場 → 昜 → 丂
- **definition:** breath
- **pinyin:** kǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts exhaled air; breath or vapor
  - **interpretation:** 丂(kǎo, "exhaled air") is traditionally depicted as the shape of breath or vapor being exhaled, characterizing the concept of air being expelled from the mouth. This led to meanings associated with breath or something that has escaped into the air.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 丂](@media/glyph4e02.png)
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場 → 昜 → 彡
- **definition:** rays of light
- **pinyin:** xiǎn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts three strands of hair ->
    - used to indicate three light rays in certain contexts
  - **interpretation:** 彡(shān, "rays") originally depicted strands of hair but also came to represent light rays, reflecting a change in symbolic meaning over time. Its use as a representation of 'ornament' and in characters like 昜 and 參 highlights its versatility in indicating rays or decorative elements.
- **examples:**
  - 天( )空( )洒(灑)下( )金( )色( )的( )彡( )，大( )地( )迎( )来(來)温(溫)暖( )。
    - Tiānkōng sǎ xià jīnsè de shān, dàdì yíng lái wēnnuǎn.
    - The sky showers golden rays, and the earth welcomes warmth.
  - 晨( )曦( )中( )的( )彡( )闪(閃)耀( )着(著)希( )望( )。
    - Chénxī zhōng de shān shǎnyào zhe xīwàng.
    - The rays in the morning light shine with hope.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 彡](@media/glyph5f61.png)

## parking lot

## 菜( )单(單)
---
## menu
### càidān
---
- **traditional:** 菜單
- **definition:** menu
- **pinyin:** càidān
- **components:**
  - 菜
    - cài
    - vegetable; dish
  - 单(單)
    - dān
    - list
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 菜 (cài, "vegetable; dish") + 单(單) (dān, "list") =
    - 菜( )單(单) (càidān, "menu")
  - **interpretation:** The word 菜( )單(单) (càidān) combines 菜 (cài, "vegetable; dish") which refers to food or dishes, and 单(單) (dān, "list") indicating a list or record. Together, it logically refers to a list of dishes, or a menu. This reflects the exact purpose of a menu as it provides a list of dishes available to choose from.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)给(給)我( )看( )菜( )单(單)，我( )想( )点(點)一( )道( )菜( )。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ kàn càidān, wǒ xiǎng diǎn yī dào cài.
    - Please show me the menu, I want to order a dish.
  - 这(這)里(裡)的( )菜( )单(單)很( )丰(豐)富( )。
    - Zhèlǐ de càidān hěn fēngfù.
    - The menu here is very diverse.
### 菜( )单(單) → 菜
- **definition:** vegetable; dish
- **pinyin:** cài
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass; plant
  - 采
    - cǎi
    - pluck
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艹 (meaning 'grass; plant') + phonetic 采 (sound) ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** The character 菜 (cài, 'vegetable; dish; cuisine; greens') combines the semantic 艹, representing plant life or vegetation, with 采 (cǎi), which provides the phonetic element. The semantic 艹 indicates that the meanings are related to plants or vegetation, while the phonetic 采 contributes to the character's pronunciation.
- **examples:**
  - 每( )道( )菜( )都( )有( )独(獨)特( )的( )风(風)味( )。
    - Měi dào cài dōu yǒu dútè de fēngwèi.
    - Every dish has a unique flavor.
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)吃( )绿(綠)色( )的( )蔬( )菜( )，因( )为(為)它( )们(們)对(對)健( )康( )有( )益( )。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī lǜsè de shūcài, yīnwèi tāmen duì jiànkāng yǒuyì.
    - I like eating green vegetables because they are good for health.
  - 中餐有很多不同的菜色，从(從)辣( )到( )甜( )都( )有( )。
    - Zhōngcān yǒu hěn duō bùtóng de càisè, cóng là dào tián dōu yǒu.
    - Chinese cuisine has many different dishes, ranging from spicy to sweet.
- **historical forms:**

### 菜( )单(單) → 菜 → 艹
- **definition:** grass; plant
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )写(寫)字( )时(時)用( )艹( )作( )草( )字( )的( )偏( )旁( )。
    - Tā xiězì shí yòng cǎo zuò cǎozì de piānpáng.
    - He uses '艹' as the radical for grass in his characters.
  - 春( )天( )到( )来(來)时(時)，艹( )生( )长(長)得( )很( )快( )。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, cǎo shēngzhǎng de hěn kuài.
    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.
### 菜( )单(單) → 菜 → 采(採)
- **traditional:** 採
- **definition:** pluck
- **pinyin:** cǎi
- **components:**
  - 扌(手)
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 扌(hand) + 采(to pick) =
    - action of picking with hand ->
    - pluck
  - **interpretation:** The character 採 represents the action of picking or plucking using one's hand. The semantic component 扌(shǒu, "hand") indicates the action being performed, while 采(cǎi, "to pick") serves the phonetic role. Over time, 采 was retained in simplified usage, whereas 採 is used traditionally.
  - **simplification:** 采 is a simplification of 採 by using the original form that omits the 手 hand radical for brevity while retaining the phonetic element.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )喜( )欢(歡)在( )花( )园(園)里(裡)采(採)花( )。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài huāyuán lǐ cǎi huā.
    - She likes to pluck flowers in the garden.
  - 我( )们(們)去( )山( )上( )采(採)草( )药(藥)。
    - Wǒmen qù shān shàng cǎi cǎoyào.
    - We go to the mountains to pluck herbs.
  - 他( )在( )果( )园(園)里(裡)采(採)苹(蘋)果( )。
    - Tā zài guǒyuán lǐ cǎi píngguǒ.
    - He plucks apples in the orchard.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 采](@media/glyph91c7.png)
### 菜( )单(單) → 菜 → 采(採) → 扌
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stylized hand. The top stroke is the bent middle finger, and the horizontal strokes each represent two fingers.
  - **interpretation:** 扌 is a simplified form of 手 (shǒu, 'hand'), retaining the key elements that visually represent a human hand. It is commonly used as a component in other characters related to hand actions.
  - **simplification:** 扌 is derived as a cursive or shorthand form of 手 (shǒu, 'hand'), making it easier to incorporate into complex characters as a radical or component.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )伸( )出( )扌(手)接( )住( )了( )飞(飛)来(來)的( )球( )。
    - Tā shēnchū shǒu jiēzhù le fēilái de qiú.
    - He stretched out his hand to catch the flying ball.
  - 她( )用( )扌(手)制(製)作( )美( )丽(麗)的( )陶( )艺(藝)，展( )现(現)她( )的( )匠( )心( )。
    - Tā yòng shǒu zhìzuò měilì de táoyì, zhǎnxiàn tā de jiàngxīn.
    - She used her hand to create beautiful pottery, showcasing her craftsmanship.
  - 艺(藝)术(術)家( )细(細)心( )雕( )刻( )扌(手)的( )每( )一( )细(細)节(節)。
    - Yìshùjiā xìxīn diāokè shǒu de měiyī xìjié.
    - The artist meticulously carved every detail of the hand.
### 菜( )单(單) → 单(單)
- **traditional:** 單
- **definition:** list
- **pinyin:** dān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Y-shaped wooden stick with stones ->
    - hunting or war weapon ->
    - resemblance to 中 ->
    - stylized to 田
  - **interpretation:** Initially depicting a Y-shaped weapon with stones suggesting a hunting tool, the character evolved visually, resembling a pole or stick (中), later taking a form similar to 田. This innovative stylization reveals its original purpose as a practical tool for warfare or hunting, thereby informing its association with tasks and lists in the modern sense.
  - **simplification:** 单(單): The character was simplified by removing the complex elements within 田, reducing it to a more direct form that still suggests the idea of a singular, straightforward entity akin to a list.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)给(給)我( )一( )张(張)清( )单(單)。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ yī zhāng qīngdān.
    - Please give me a list.
  - 他( )列( )出( )了( )需( )要( )购(購)买(買)的( )物( )品( )清( )单(單)。
    - Tā liè chūle xūyào gòumǎi de wùpǐn qīngdān.
    - He made a list of items to purchase.
  - 她( )准(準)备(備)了( )一( )份( )客( )人( )的( )名( )单(單)。
    - Tā zhǔnbèi le yī fèn kèrén de míngdān.
    - She prepared a list of guests.

## thirsty
### kě
---
- **definition:** thirsty
- **pinyin:** kě
- **components:**
  - 氵(水)
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 曷
    - hé
    - why, what
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 氵(水) (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic 曷 (hé) ->
    - meaning: dry, exhausted (of water)
  - **interpretation:** The character 渴(kě, "thirsty") combines the semantic component 氵(shuǐ, "water"), essential for life and quenching thirst, with the phonetic component 曷(hé), which indicates the sound. The concept of being dry or exhausted due to a lack of water leads to the meaning of 'thirst'.
- **examples:**
  - 他很渴，所以喝了一大瓶水。
    - Tā hěn kě, suǒyǐ hēle yī dà píng shuǐ.
    - He was very thirsty, so he drank a big bottle of water.
  - 运(運)动(動)后(後)，我( )总(總)是( )感( )到( )渴( )。
    - Yùndòng hòu, wǒ zǒng shì gǎndào kě.
    - After exercising, I always feel thirsty.
  - 她渴了，需( )要( )喝( )点(點)水( )。
    - Tā kě le, xūyào hē diǎn shuǐ.
    - She is thirsty and needs to drink some water.
- **historical forms:**

### 渴 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字( )中( )偏( )旁( )氵( )，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快( )戏(戲)水( )。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.

    - meaning

The semantic part suggests an interrogative aspect, as if questioning speech or something said. Thus, it forms the basis for meanings like 'why' and 'what' that indicate inquiries or questioning.

## bear
### xióng
---
- **definition:** bear
- **pinyin:** xióng
- **components:**
  - 能
    - néng
    - able
  - 炎
    - yán
    - flame
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 能 (néng, "able") + abbreviated phonetic 炎 (yán, "flame") ->
    - original representation of an onomatopoetic word for flaming ->
    - borrowed for the word 'bear'
  - **interpretation:** Originally, 熊(xióng, "bear") depicted the sound of flames raging, with 炎 (yán, "flame") as the sound component and 能 (néng, "able") representing the original semantic concept of a familiar powerful presence, later shifting to mean 'bear' when 能 (néng, "bear") was borrowed for the animal name.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)熊( )看( )起( )来(來)很( )友( )好( )。
    - Zhè ge xióng kàn qǐlái hěn yǒuhǎo.
    - This bear looks friendly.
  - 熊( )喜( )欢(歡)住( )在( )森( )林( )里(裡)。
    - Xióng xǐhuān zhù zài sēnlín lǐ.
    - Bears like to live in the forest.
  - 当(當)我( )在( )山( )上( )徒( )步( )时(時)，我看到了一个熊。
    - Dāng wǒ zài shān shàng túbù shí, wǒ kàn dào le yī gè xióng.
    - When I was hiking in the mountains, I saw a bear.
- **historical forms:**

### 熊 → 能
- **definition:** able
- **pinyin:** néng
- **components:**
  - 匕
    - bǐ
    - spoon
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bear: two paws stylized as 匕 (bǐ, "spoon") + face/mouth stylized as 月 (yuè, "moon")
  - **interpretation:** The character 能(néng), originally meant to represent a bear, combines elements stylized as paws and a face to visually convey an animal's features. Over time, this depiction of a bear has lent its phonetic value to words associated with ability and energy.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)座( )桥(橋)能( )承( )受( )大( )风(風)。
    - Zhè zuò qiáo néng chéngshòu dà fēng.
    - This bridge can bear strong winds.
  - 他( )能( )承( )受( )巨( )大( )压(壓)力( )。
    - Tā néng chéngshòu jùdà yālì.
    - He can bear tremendous pressure.
  - 这(這)台( )电(電)脑(腦)能( )运(運)行( )复(複)杂(雜)程( )序( )，满(滿)足( )现(現)代( )需( )求( )。
    - Zhè tái diànnǎo néng yùnxíng fùzá chéngxù, mǎnzú xiàndài xūqiú.
    - This computer can run complex programs, meeting modern needs.
- **historical forms:**

### 熊 → 能 → 匕
- **definition:** spoon
- **pinyin:** bǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a spoon
  - **interpretation:** The character 匕(bǐ, 'cane') originally depicts a spoon, which has a similar shape to the character itself. It is unrelated to the meanings of 'walking cane', 'knife', or 'person', which appear in other characters with similar forms.
- **examples:**
  - 古( )时(時)候( )的( )老( )人( )常( )用( )匕( )支( )撑(撐)。

  - 他( )拄( )着(著)匕( )，在( )公( )园(園)里(裏)散( )步( )。

    - He walked in the park with a cane.

### 熊 → 能 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜( )空( )挂(掛)着(著)明( )月( )。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.

    - two fires together ->
    - flame, inflammation
  - **interpretation:** The character combines two 火 (huǒ, 'fire') symbols, emphasizing an intense or extensive fire. This conveys the meanings of 'flame' and 'inflammation', as both involve a spreading or intensified heat.

### 熊 → 炎 → 火
- **definition:** fire
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames rising from a fire
  - **interpretation:** The character 火 (huǒ, "fire") visually represents flames flickering upwards, which intuitively conveys the essence of fire. This simple depiction is an effective way to capture the dynamic and essential nature of fire.
- **examples:**
  - 火( )在( )壁( )炉(爐)中( )熊( )熊( )燃( )烧(燒)。

## 害怕
---
## to be afraid
### hàipà
---
- **definition:** to be afraid
- **pinyin:** hàipà
- **components:**
  - 害
    - hài
    - harm
  - 怕
    - pà
    - fear
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 害 (hài, "harm") + 怕 (pà, "fear") =
    - to experience fear from a potential harm, leading to the feeling of being afraid
  - **interpretation:** 害 (hài, "harm") suggests the presence of something that could cause trouble or injury, while 怕 (pà, "fear") represents the emotional response to such a threat. Together, they indicate the feeling of being afraid, as one experiences fear when there is a potential for harm or danger.
- **examples:**
  - 她害怕黑暗。
    - Tā hàipà hēi'àn.
    - She is afraid of the dark.
  - 他( )不( )再( )害( )怕( )说(說)话(話)。
    - Tā bùzài hàipà shuōhuà.
    - He is no longer afraid to speak.
  - 孩( )子( )们(們)对(對)吠( )叫( )的( )狗( )感( )到( )害( )怕( )。
    - Háizimen duì fèijiào de gǒu gǎndào hàipà.
    - The children are afraid of the barking dog.
### 害怕 → 害
- **definition:** harm
- **pinyin:** hài
- **components:**
  - 宀
    - mián
    - house
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 丯
    - xiè
    - sound of 廨
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 宀 (house) + semantic 口 (mouth) + phonetic 丯 (sound of 廨) ->
    - harm
  - **interpretation:** The character 害(hài, "harm") combines the idea of a structure (represented by 宀) as a place where harm or impact occurs, often internal or hidden, with a mouth (口) perhaps suggesting exposure or sharing of harm, with a phonetic component 丯 to provide the sound. This creates the notion of causing harm or trouble, as if something undesirable is shared or released within a space.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )不( )小( )心( )摔( )倒( )，害( )我( )也( )被( )绊(絆)倒( )了( )。
    - Tā bù xiǎoxīn shuāi dǎo，hài wǒ yě bèi bàn dǎo le。
    - He accidentally fell and caused me to trip as well.
  - 吸( )烟(煙)对(對)健( )康( )有( )害( )。
    - Xī yān duì jiànkāng yǒu hài。
    - Smoking is harmful to health.
  - 这(這)个(個)决(決)定( )可( )能( )会(會)害( )很( )多( )人( )受( )影( )响(響)。
    - Zhège juédìng kěnéng huì hài hěn duō rén shòu yǐngxiǎng。
    - This decision might harm many people.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 害](@media/glyph5bb3.png)
### 害怕 → 害 → 宀
- **definition:** house
- **pinyin:** mián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a house with four walls ->
    - roof
  - **interpretation:** 宀(mián, "roof") is a pictogram representing a house with four walls. It emphasizes an enclosed space, distinguishing it from similar structures like 广(guǎng, "broad") which depicts a building with three walls. This makes 宀 a logical choice for representing a roof in various characters.
- **examples:**
  - 含( )有( )宀( )的( )汉(漢)字( )代( )表( )家( )的( )温(溫)暖( )。
    - Hán yǒu mián de hànzì dàibiǎo jiā de wēnnuǎn.
    - Chinese characters that include the radical '宀' represent the warmth of home.
  - 屋( )顶(頂)遮( )风(風)挡(擋)雨( )，家( )园(園)散( )发(發)温(溫)馨( )。
    - Wūdǐng zhē fēng dǎng yǔ, jiāyuán sànfā wēnxīn.
    - The roof shields from wind and rain, and the home radiates warmth.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 宀](@media/glyph5b80.png)
### 害怕 → 害 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 害怕 → 害 → 丯
- **definition:** sound of 廨
- **pinyin:** xiè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts something carved/engraved ->
    - proto-form of 㓞 (carving tool); unrelated to 丰 (abundance or plenty)
  - **interpretation:** The character 丯 (jiè, 'aid') is originally a pictogram showing an object that is carved or engraved, suggesting its connection to manual or artistic intervention. This carved form visually represents the concept of aid by implying attentiveness or deliberate shaping. It serves as a proto-form for 㓞, which indicates the act of carving or cutting, thereby aligning with the notion of aid provided through skill and craft.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 丯](@media/glyph4e2f.png)
### 害怕 → 怕
- **definition:** fear
- **pinyin:** pà
- **components:**
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
  - 白
    - bái
    - white
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 心 (heart) + phonetic 白 (bái) ->
    - fear
  - **interpretation:** The character 怕 (pà, "fear") combines the semantic component 心 (xīn, "heart") with the phonetic component 白 (bái). The heart component implies an emotional state or feeling, and when combined with 白, which provides the sound, it suggests the feeling of fear or being afraid. The heart as the center of emotions is intuitively associated with fear.
- **examples:**
  - 他怕黑。
    - Tā pà hēi.
    - He is afraid of the dark.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)怕( )我( )们(們)饿(餓)了( )，给(給)我( )们(們)准(準)备(備)了( )很( )多( )食( )物( )。
    - Māmā pà wǒmen è le, gěi wǒmen zhǔnbèi le hěn duō shíwù.
    - Mom is afraid we might be hungry, so she prepared a lot of food for us.
  - 小( )孩( )子( )们(們)怕( )打( )针(針)，所( )以( )医(醫)生( )很( )温(溫)柔( )。
    - Xiǎo háizi men pà dǎzhēn, suǒyǐ yīshēng hěn wēnróu.
    - Children are afraid of injections, so the doctor is very gentle.
### 害怕 → 怕 → 心
- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a heart
  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, "heart") originally depicted the shape of an actual heart, representing thoughts, emotions, and the core of a person. Over time, it has become highly stylized, but it continues to convey the notion of the heart as the center of emotions and consciousness.
- **examples:**
  - 她的心一( )直( )都( )在( )帮(幫)助( )别(別)人( )。
    - Tā de xīn yīzhí dōu zài bāngzhù biérén.
    - Her heart is always in helping others.
  - 在城市的中心，有( )一( )个(個)美( )丽(麗)的( )公( )园(園)。
    - Zài chéngshì de zhōngxīn, yǒu yí gè měilì de gōngyuán.
    - At the center of the city, there is a beautiful park.
  - 对(對)于(於)许(許)多( )人( )来(來)说(說)，家庭是生活的核心。
    - Duìyú xǔduō rén lái shuō, jiātíng shì shēnghuó de héxīn.
    - For many people, family is the core of life.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 心](@media/glyph5fc3.png)
### 害怕 → 怕 → 白
- **definition:** white
- **pinyin:** bái
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts an acorn ->
    - white from the color of acorn's inside
  - **interpretation:** The character 白(bái, "white") is thought to depict an acorn, as suggested by its use in words related to oak and acorns. The character's meaning of "white" is likely derived from the white color of an acorn's interior.
- **examples:**
  - 白( )色( )是( )我( )最( )喜( )欢(歡)的( )颜(顏)色( )。
    - Báisè shì wǒ zuì xǐhuān de yánsè.
    - White is my favorite color.
  - 他( )的( )头(頭)发(髮)已( )经(經)全( )白( )了( )。
    - Tā de tóufà yǐjīng quán bái le.
    - His hair has turned completely white.
  - 在( )阳(陽)光( )下( )，白( )沙( )滩(灘)显(顯)得( )格( )外( )美( )丽(麗)。
    - Zài yángguāng xià, bái shātān xiǎnde géwài měilì.
    - In the sunlight, the white sandy beach looks especially beautiful.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 白](@media/glyph767d.png)

## 棵(樖)
---
## measure word for trees and plants
### kē
---
- **traditional:** 樖
- **definition:** measure word for trees and plants
- **pinyin:** kē
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood; tree
  - 可
    - kě
    - can; may
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, "wood; tree") + phonetic 可 (kě) ->
    - meaning measure word for trees and plants
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 木 (mù, "wood; tree"), indicating its relation to trees and plants, with 可 (kě) for its phonetic component. The semantic 木 reinforces the association with objects made of or related to wood, like trees and plants.
  - **simplification:** Simplified as 棵 by reducing the complexity of certain strokes in 樖, keeping the tree radical for semantic clarity while using 可 for phonetic consistency.
- **examples:**
  - 院( )子( )里(裡)有( )一( )棵( )大( )树(樹)。
    - Yuànzi lǐ yǒu yī kē dà shù.
    - There is a big tree in the yard.
  - 我( )种(種)了( )一( )棵( )苹(蘋)果( )树(樹)，它( )已( )经(經)开(開)花( )了( )。
    - Wǒ zhòngle yī kē píngguǒshù, tā yǐjīng kāihuā le.
    - I planted an apple tree, and it has already blossomed.
  - 花( )园(園)里(裡)有( )几(幾)棵( )玫( )瑰( )花( )，它( )们(們)开(開)得( )很( )漂( )亮( )。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu jǐ kē méiguīhuā, tāmen kāi de hěn piàoliang.
    - There are several rose bushes in the garden, and they bloom beautifully.
### 棵(樖) → 木
- **definition:** wood; tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把( )椅( )子( )的( )主( )要( )材( )料( )是( )木( )。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
### 棵(樖) → 可
- **definition:** can; may
- **pinyin:** kě
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 丂
    - kǎo
    - exhaled air
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic: 丂 (kǎo) =
    - reference to exhaled air "to sing" ->
    - capability to perform actions
  - **interpretation:** This character combines the semantic element 口 (kǒu, "mouth") with the phonetic 丂 (kǎo), referencing exhaling or vocal actions like singing, which suggests expressing capability or permission.
- **examples:**
  - 你( )可( )尝(嘗)试(試)一( )下( )新( )方( )法( )。
    - Nǐ kě chángshì yīxià xīn fāngfǎ.
    - You may try a new method.
  - 此( )事( )虽(雖)难(難)，你( )可( )坚(堅)持( )到( )底( )。
    - Cǐ shì suī nán, nǐ kě jiānchí dàodǐ.
    - Although this matter is difficult, you may persist to the end.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 可](@media/glyph53ef.png)
### 棵(樖) → 可 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 棵(樖) → 可 → 丂
- **definition:** exhaled air
- **pinyin:** kǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts exhaled air; breath or vapor
  - **interpretation:** 丂(kǎo, "exhaled air") is traditionally depicted as the shape of breath or vapor being exhaled, characterizing the concept of air being expelled from the mouth. This led to meanings associated with breath or something that has escaped into the air.
- **historical forms:**

## 累(纍)
---
## tired
### lèi
---
- **traditional:** 纍
- **definition:** tired
- **pinyin:** lèi
- **components:**
  - 畾
    - lěi
    - stacked fields
  - 糸
    - sī
    - silk; thread
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 畾 (lěi, "stacked fields") + 糸 (sī, "silk; thread") =
    - representation of binding with silk threads ->
    - evolved meaning of 'rope; to bind' ->
    - eventual simplification to 累 (lèi, "tired")
  - **interpretation:** The character 纍 (lěi, "bind") originally depicted stacked fields with threads used for binding or tying. The use of 畾 for the fields and 糸 for silk reflects this original purpose. The modern association with 'tired' is a semantic shift away from the original sense of binding, illustrating how meanings evolve over time.
  - **simplification:** Simplified as 累 (lèi) by reducing the structure of 纍 to the essential phonetic and semantic components.
- **examples:**
  - 工作了一整天，我( )觉(覺)得( )很( )累( )。
    - Gōngzuòle yī zhěng tiān, wǒ juédé hěn lèi.
    - After working all day, I feel very tired.
  - 孩( )子( )们(們)一( )天( )的( )玩( )耍( )，让(讓)他( )们(們)精( )疲( )力( )竭( )。
    - Háizimen yītiān de wánshuǎ, ràng tāmen jīngpílìjié.
    - The day's play exhausted the children.
  - 我累了，需要休息一下。
    - Wǒ lèile, xūyào xiūxi yīxià.
    - I'm tired and need to rest a bit.
### 累(纍) → 畾
- **definition:** stacked fields
- **pinyin:** lěi
- **components:**
  - 田
    - tián
    - field
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 田 (tián, "field") triplicated =
    - stacked fields
  - **interpretation:** The character 畾(lěi, "stacked fields") visually represents the concept of multiple fields stacked or laid alongside each other by repeating the field character 田 (tián, "field") three times, emphasizing multiplicity or accumulation.
### 累(纍) → 畾 → 田
- **definition:** field
- **pinyin:** tián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a field divided into four sections
  - **interpretation:** The character 田(tián, 'field') visually represents a field with sections, indicating its agricultural use and importance in ancient times.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民( )在( )田( )里(裡)耕( )作( )。
    - Nóngmín zài tián lǐ gēngzuò.
    - The farmer works in the field.
  - 那( )边(邊)的( )田( )长(長)满(滿)了( )庄(莊)稼( )，农(農)民( )收( )获(穫)忙( )碌( )。
    - Nàbiān de tián cháng mǎn le zhuāngjià, nóngmín shōuhuò mánglù.
    - The field over there is full of crops, and the farmer is busy harvesting.
  - 秋( )收( )时(時)节(節)，人( )们(們)忙( )于(於)收( )割( )田( )里(裡)的( )稻( )谷( )。
    - Qiūshōu shíjié, rénmen máng yú shōugē tián lǐ de dàogǔ.
    - During the harvest season, people are busy reaping the rice in the fields.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 田](@media/glyph7530.png)
### 累(纍) → 糸
- **definition:** silk; thread
- **pinyin:** sī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )手( )工( )制(製)作( )了( )一( )条(條)漂( )亮( )的( )丝(絲)巾( )。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.
    - She handcrafted a beautiful silk scarf.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)图(圖)必( )须(須)用( )细(細)糸( )画(畫)出( )来(來)。
    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.
  - 我( )们(們)参(參)观(觀)了( )古( )代( )的( )织(織)布( )技( )术(術)，对(對)丝(絲)绸(綢)制(製)作( )产(產)生( )了( )兴(興)趣( )。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.
    - We visited ancient weaving techniques and developed an interest in silk production.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 糸](@media/glyph7cf8.png)

## 树(樹)
---
## tree
### shù
---
- **traditional:** 樹
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** shù
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 尌
    - shù
    - to plant a tree
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Originally 尌 (phonetic, 'to plant a tree') + 木 (mù, 'tree') added for clarity ->
    - tree
  - **interpretation:** 樹 combines the semantic 木 (mù, 'tree') with the phonetic 尌 to convey the meaning of 'tree'. The phonetic element 尌 originally depicted the act of planting a tree, and 木 emphasizes the botanical aspect.
  - **simplification:** 壴 (壴, 'drum or musical instrument') was replaced by 又 (又, 'again') to simplify stroke count, losing the original phonetic connection in favor of visual simplicity.
- **examples:**
  - 公( )园(園)里(裡)的( )树(樹)很( )高( )大( )。
    - Gōngyuán lǐ de shù hěn gāodà.
    - The trees in the park are very tall.
  - 秋( )天( )时(時)树(樹)叶(葉)变(變)黄(黃)。
    - Qiūtiān shí shùyè biàn huáng.
    - In autumn, the tree leaves turn yellow.
  - 那( )棵( )老( )树(樹)见(見)证(證)了( )许(許)多( )历(歷)史( )。
    - Nà kē lǎo shù jiànzhèngle xǔduō lìshǐ.
    - That old tree has witnessed a lot of history.
### 树(樹) → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把( )椅( )子( )的( )主( )要( )材( )料( )是( )木( )。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
### 树(樹) → 尌
- **definition:** to plant a tree
- **pinyin:** shù
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - hand
  - 豆
    - dòu
    - drum
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 木 (mù, 'tree') + 寸 (cùn, 'hand') =
    - to plant a tree ->
    - 豆 (dòu, used phonetic) added later
  - **interpretation:** The character 尌 originally depicted planting a tree with a hand, represented by 木 (mù, 'tree') and 寸 (cùn, 'hand'). A phonetic component 豆 (dòu) was added later to distinguish its meaning, although in modern forms, 木 and 豆 have visually merged into 壴.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 尌](@media/glyph5c0c.png)
### 树(樹) → 尌 → 寸
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)块(塊)布( )每( )一( )寸( )都( )是( )精( )心( )制(製)作( )。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用( )卷( )尺( )量( )一( )寸( )，每( )一( )寸( )数(數)据(據)都( )准(準)确(確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 寸](@media/glyph5bf8.png)
### 树(樹) → 尌 → 豆
- **definition:** drum
- **pinyin:** dòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a container ->
    - borrowed phonetically for the plant name
  - **interpretation:** The character 豆(dòu, 'drum') originally depicted a type of container. It was later borrowed for its phonetic value to represent the plant name 'bean', distinguishing it from a container. This transition indicates how the physical shape of the container, resembling a drum or storage pot, facilitated a phonetic borrowing.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )们(們)在( )课(課)堂( )上( )学(學)习(習)如( )何( )制(製)作( )豆( )。
    - Wǒmen zài kètáng shàng xuéxí rúhé zhìzuò dòu.
    - We are learning how to make drums in class.
  - 村( )庄(莊)里(裡)有( )一( )个(個)古( )老( )的( )豆( )，它( )的( )声(聲)音( )很( )有( )魅( )力( )。
    - Cūnzhuāng lǐ yǒu yí gè gǔlǎo de dòu, tā de shēngyīn hěn yǒu mèilì.
    - There is an ancient drum in the village, and its sound is captivating.
  - 音( )乐(樂)会(會)以( )豆( )声(聲)开(開)场(場)，让(讓)观(觀)众(眾)立( )刻( )沉(沈)浸( )在( )气(氣)氛( )中( )。
    - Yīnyuèhuì yǐ dòu shēng kāichǎng, ràng guānzhòng lìkè chénjìn zài qìfēn zhōng.
    - The concert opened with the sound of drums, immersing the audience in the atmosphere immediately.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 豆](@media/glyph8c46.png)

## 死
