## to die
### sǐ
---
- **definition:** to die
- **pinyin:** sǐ
- **components:**
  - 歹
    - dǎi
    - carcass
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 歹 (dǎi, "carcass") + 人 (rén, "person") =
    - person with remains ->
    - death
  - **interpretation:** The character 死(sǐ, "to die") combines 歹 (dǎi, "carcass") indicating death with 人 (rén, "person") to symbolize a deceased person, highlighting its association with human mortality.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )决(決)心( )大( )到( )不( )怕( )死( )。
    - Tā de juéxīn dà dào bù pà sǐ.
    - His determination is so strong that he is not afraid to die.
  - 战(戰)场(場)上( )，他( )见(見)到( )许(許)多( )勇( )士( )倒( )下( )死( )去( )。
    - Zhànchǎng shàng, tā jiàndào xǔduō yǒngshì dǎoxià sǐqù.
    - On the battlefield, he saw many brave warriors fall and die.
  - 传(傳)说(說)中( )，英( )雄( )死( )后(後)获(獲)得( )永( )生( )。
    - Chuánshuō zhōng, yīngxióng sǐhòu huòdé yǒngshēng.
    - According to legend, heroes gain eternal life after death.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 死](@media/glyph6b7b.png)
### 死 → 歹
- **definition:** carcass
- **pinyin:** dǎi
- **components:**
  - 歺
    - è
    - variant form of 歹
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts human remains ->
    - related to 歺 as an intermediate variant
  - **interpretation:** 歹(dǎi, "carcass") is a pictorial representation of human remains. The character preserves an ancient form that visually suggests its meaning, and is related to the intermediate variant 歺.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )在( )树(樹)林( )中( )发(發)现(現)一( )具( )歹( )。
    - Tā zài shùlín zhōng fāxiàn yī jù dǎi.
    - He discovered a carcass in the woods.
  - 雨( )后(後)天( )晴( )时(時)，村( )边(邊)野( )地( )露( )出( )一( )具( )歹( )。
    - Yǔ hòu tiān qíng shí, cūn biān yě dì lù chū yī jù dǎi.
    - After the rain, when the weather cleared, a carcass appeared on the village outskirts.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 歹](@media/glyph6b79.png)
### 死 → 歹 → 歺
- **definition:** variant form of 歹
- **pinyin:** è
- **components:**
  - 歹
    - dǎi
    - bad; death
  - 餐
    - cān
    - meal
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts human remains ->
    - variant form of 歹 (dǎi, "bad; death")
  - **interpretation:** The character 歺 evolved as a variant of the character 歹 (dǎi, "bad; death"), depicting human remains. The top component in characters like 餐 (cān, "meal") historically retained the intermediate form of 歺, showcasing its connection to the idea of decay or death.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)是( )一( )种(種)罕( )见(見)的( )古( )字( )。
    - Zhè shì yī zhǒng hǎnjiàn de gǔ zì.
    - This is a rare ancient character.
  - “歺( )”这(這)个(個)字( )在( )现(現)代( )汉(漢)语(語)中( )很( )少( )使( )用( )。
    - “È” zhège zì zài xiàndài hànyǔ zhōng hěn shǎo shǐyòng.
    - The character “歺” is rarely used in modern Chinese.
  - 我( )们(們)老( )师(師)介( )绍(紹)了( )“歺( )”字( )的( )起( )源( )。
    - Wǒmen lǎoshī jièshàole “è” zì de qǐyuán.
    - Our teacher introduced the origin of the character “歺”.
### 死 → 歹 → 歺 → 餐
- **definition:** meal
- **pinyin:** cān
- **components:**
  - 𣦼
    - cán
    - approach, converge
  - 食
    - shí
    - to eat
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic: 𣦼 (cán) + Semantic: 食 (shí, "to eat") =
    - 'to swallow' ->
    - evolves to 'meal'
  - **interpretation:** The character 餐(cān) uses 𣦼(cán) to convey sound and 食(shí, "to eat") for meaning, originally depicting the action of swallowing, which naturally extends to refer to meals.
- **examples:**
  - 我今天享用了美味的晚餐。
    - Wǒ jīntiān xiǎngyòngle měiwèi de wǎncān.
    - I enjoyed a delicious dinner today.
  - 我忙了一天，终(終)于(於)坐( )下( )来(來)享( )用( )餐( )。
    - Wǒ mángle yītiān, zhōngyú zuò xiàlái xiǎngyòng cān.
    - After a busy day, I finally sat down to enjoy a meal.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 餐](@media/glyph9910.png)
### 死 → 歹 → 歺 → 餐 → 𣦼
- **definition:** approach, converge
- **pinyin:** cán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant
  - **description:** Variant of 𣦻. This form shares its meaning and serves as another written version
  - **interpretation:** The character 𣦼 is a variant form, meaning it provides an alternative visual representation of the same concept as 𣦻, which is 'approach, converge'. It likely maintains the same structural components as 𣦻 but differs visually.
### 死 → 歹 → 歺 → 餐 → 食
- **definition:** to eat
- **pinyin:** shí
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - jí
    - assemble
  - 𠊊
    - jí
    - bowl with stand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Pictogram
  - **description:** 亼 (jí, "assemble") over a pictographic bowl of rice on a stand, symbolized by 𠊊 (jí, "bowl with stand")
  - **interpretation:** Initially, the character 食 (shí, "eat") visually represented a mouth over a bowl of rice, conveying the act of eating or a meal intuitively through this imagery.
- **examples:**
  - 他食得很快。
    - Tā shí dé hěn kuài.
    - He eats very quickly.
  - 我( )准(準)备(備)午( )食( )，与(與)朋( )友( )共( )享( )佳( )肴(餚)。
    - Wǒ zhǔnbèi wǔ shí, yǔ péngyǒu gòngxiǎng jiāyáo.
    - I am preparing lunch to share a delicious meal with my friends.
  - 民( )以( )食( )为(為)天( )。
    - Mín yǐ shí wéi tiān.
    - Food is regarded as the most important element for the people.
### 死 → 歹 → 歺 → 餐 → 食 → 亼
- **definition:** assemble
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)
### 死 → 歹 → 歺 → 餐 → 食 → 𠊊
- **definition:** bowl with stand
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - jí
    - mouth
  - 皀
    - jí
    - bowl of rice on a stand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 亼 (mouth) over 皀 (bowl of rice on a stand) ->
    - depicts a bowl with a stand
  - **interpretation:** The character 𠊊 visually represents a mouth above a bowl of rice on a stand, indicating a utensil or vessel used for holding food. This image directly links to the idea of a 'bowl with stand.' The component 皀 specifically conveys the idea of a container or bowl elevated, which situates its primary meaning in the context of serving or holding food.
### 死 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )个(個)好( )人( )。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每( )个(個)人( )都( )有( )责(責)任( )，为(為)社( )会(會)作( )出( )贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心( )灵(靈)获(獲)得( )了( )成( )长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.

## 装(裝)
---
## to pretend; to act as
### zhūang
---
- **traditional:** 裝
- **definition:** to pretend; to act as
- **pinyin:** zhūang
- **components:**
  - 衣
    - yī
    - clothes
  - 壯
    - zhuàng
    - strong; robust
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 衣 (yī, "clothes") + phonetic 壯 (zhuàng) ->
    - clothing-related action or concept
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 衣 (yī, "clothes") as the semantic part suggests a connection to clothing or dress, while 壯 (zhuàng) provides the pronunciation. The core idea of 'clothing' extends metaphorically to 'pretending' or 'acting as,' similar to dressing up or adopting a role.
  - **simplification:** 装(裝): The traditional character 裝 was simplified by removing the semantic 衣 component, streamlining the character for easier writing.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )装(裝)得( )很( )开(開)心( )。
    - Tā zhuāng de hěn kāixīn.
    - He pretended to be very happy.
  - 我( )不( )想( )装(裝)不( )知( )道( )，因( )此( )直( )接( )问(問)了( )他( )。
    - Wǒ bù xiǎng zhuāng bù zhīdào, yīncǐ zhíjiē wèn le tā.
    - I didn't want to pretend not to know, so I asked him directly.
  - 有( )人( )喜( )欢(歡)在( )公( )众(衆)场(場)合( )装(裝)作( )别(別)人( )。
    - Yǒurén xǐhuān zài gōngzhòng chǎnghé zhuāng zuò biérén.
    - Some people like to pretend to be someone else in public places.
### 装(裝) → 衣
- **definition:** clothes
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a basic outline of a garment with sleeves hanging down.
  - **interpretation:** The character 衣 (yī, 'clothes') clearly resembles a simple garment, with parts representing sleeves and the body of clothing. This visual representation aligns with its meaning of 'clothes' or 'clothing.'
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)件( )衣( )很( )特( )别(別)。
    - Zhè jiàn yī hěn tè bié.
    - This piece of clothing is very special.
  - 冬( )天( )来(來)了( )，人( )们(們)换(換)上( )了( )暖( )和( )的( )衣( )。
    - Dōngtiān lái le, rénmen huàn shàng le nuǎn huó de yī.
    - Winter has arrived, and people put on warm clothes.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 衣](@media/glyph8863.png)
### 装(裝) → 壯
- **definition:** strong; robust
- **pinyin:** zhuàng
- **components:**
  - 士
    - shì
    - scholar
  - 爿
    - pán
    - bed; half of a tree trunk
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 士 (shì, "scholar") + phonetic 爿 (pán) ->
    - strong
  - **interpretation:** The character combines the semantic 士 (shì, "scholar"), associated with authority or prominence, and the phonetic component 爿 (pán), which provides the sound, to convey the idea of strength or robustness, emphasizing a strong or sturdy stature.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )看( )起( )来(來)很( )强(強)壮(壯)。
    - Tā kàn qǐlái hěn qiángzhuàng.
    - He looks very strong.
  - 这(這)栋(棟)建( )筑(築)很( )壮(壯)观(觀)。
    - Zhè dòng jiànzhù hěn zhuàngguān.
    - This building is very magnificent.
  - 经(經)过(過)锻(鍛)炼(煉)，他( )变(變)得( )更( )加( )壮(壯)实(實)。
    - Jīngguò duànliàn, tā biàn dé gèngjiā zhuàngshí.
    - After exercising, he became even stronger.
### 装(裝) → 壯 → 士
- **definition:** scholar
- **pinyin:** shì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a ritual axe, possibly made of jade ->
    - symbolized soldier ->
    - intellectual or officer over time
  - **interpretation:** The character 士(shì, 'scholar') originally depicted a ritual axe used in ceremonies, implying a person of a certain rank or status who could wield such symbols. This connection to ceremonial authority evolved to mean 'soldier' and later 'intellectual' or 'officer', roles associated with leadership and knowledge in societal hierarchies.
- **examples:**
  - 历(歷)史( )上( )，士( )被( )视(視)为(為)一( )种(種)权(權)力( )的( )象( )征(徵)。
    - Lìshǐ shàng, shì bèi shì wéi yī zhǒng quánlì de xiàngzhēng.
    - Historically, the 'shi' was seen as a symbol of power.
  - 在( )古( )代( )，只( )有( )贵(貴)族( )才( )拥(擁)有( )士( )。
    - Zài gǔdài, zhǐyǒu guìzú cái yǒngyǒu shì.
    - In ancient times, only nobles possessed the 'shi'.
  - 士( )的( )制(製)作( )材( )料( )可( )能( )是( )珍( )贵(貴)的( )金( )属(屬)。
    - Shì de zhìzuò cáiliào kěnéng shì zhēnguì de jīnshǔ.
    - The materials used to make the 'shi' might have been precious metals.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 士](@media/glyph58eb.png)
### 装(裝) → 壯 → 爿
- **definition:** bed; half of a tree trunk
- **pinyin:** pán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a bed ->
    - original form of 牀 (chuáng, "bed") ->
    - contracted form in 臧 (zāng, "possess")
  - **interpretation:** The character 爿 (pán, "bed") visually represents a bed, emphasizing its usage in denoting places for resting or sleeping. It served as the original form for the character 牀 (chuáng, "bed"), reinforcing its meaning. Additionally, in the character 臧 (zāng, "possess"), it appears as a contracted form, reflecting its historical usage in composite forms.
- **historical forms:**

## 动(動)
---
## to move
### dòng
---
- **traditional:** 動
- **definition:** to move
- **pinyin:** dòng
- **components:**
  - 力
    - lì
    - strength
  - 重
    - zhòng
    - heavy
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 力 (lì, "strength") + phonetic 重 (zhòng) ->
    - movement aided by strength ->
    - move
  - **interpretation:** The character 動 suggests using strength 力 (lì, "strength") to move something heavy, as indicated by the phonetic component 重 (zhòng, "heavy"). This conveys the concept of movement or change.
  - **simplification:** The character 動 was simplified by replacing 重 (zhòng, "heavy") with 云 (yún, "cloud") to form 动, reducing the complexity of writing.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )动(動)了( )一( )下( )椅( )子( )。
    - Tā dòng le yīxià yǐzi.
    - He moved the chair slightly.
  - 我( )的( )心( )被( )她( )的( )话(話)感( )动(動)了( )。
    - Wǒ de xīn bèi tā de huà gǎn dòng le.
    - My heart was moved by her words.
  - 天( )气(氣)一( )变(變)动(動)，就( )会(會)下( )雨( )。
    - Tiānqì yī biàn dòng, jiù huì xià yǔ.
    - As soon as the weather changes, it will rain.
### 动(動) → 力
- **definition:** strength
- **pinyin:** lì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts either an arm bending out from the side of the body, or a wooden plough
  - **interpretation:** The character 力(lì, 'strength') visually represents physical power through the image of an arm or tool, emphasizing the fundamental concept of muscular force.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )尽(盡)全( )力( )，赢(贏)得( )比( )赛(賽)。
    - Tā yòng jìn quánlì, yíng dé bǐsài.
    - He used all his strength to win the competition.
  - 他( )把( )力( )气(氣)用( )在( )学(學)习(習)上( )。
    - Tā bǎ lìqì yòng zài xuéxí shàng.
    - He applies his strength to his studies.
  - 面( )对(對)困( )难(難)，他( )毫( )不( )退( )缩(縮)，全力以赴。
    - Miànduì kùnnán, tā háo bù tuìsuō, quánlì yǐ fù.
    - Facing difficulties, he neither retreats nor gives up, but goes all out.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 力](@media/glyph529b.png)
### 动(動) → 重
- **definition:** heavy
- **pinyin:** zhòng
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - man
  - 東
    - dōng
    - bag
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "man") + 東 (dōng, "bag") =
    - a man carrying a bag ->
    - 土 (tǔ, "earth") added ->
    - symbol of load ->
    - final form
  - **interpretation:** Originally, it depicts a man carrying a bag, indicating the concept of weight. With 土 (tǔ, "earth") added to signify being grounded, it amplifies the idea of heaviness due to the man's connection to the ground or earth, suggesting substantial weight or burden. This visual representation naturally evolved into "heavy", as a person burdened by earth is weighed down.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)箱( )苹(蘋)果( )很( )重( )。
    - Zhè xiāng píngguǒ hěn zhòng.
    - This box of apples is very heavy.
  - 他的行李太重，无(無)法( )一( )个(個)人( )搬( )动(動)。
    - Tā de xíngli tài zhòng, wúfǎ yīgè rén bāndòng.
    - His luggage is too heavy to carry alone.
  - 雨( )后(後)的( )空( )气(氣)显(顯)得( )特( )别(別)重( )。
    - Yǔ hòu de kōngqì xiǎnde tèbié zhòng.
    - The air feels especially heavy after the rain.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 重](@media/glyph91cd.png)

### 动(動) → 重 → 東
- **definition:** bag
- **pinyin:** dōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bundle or bag tied at both ends
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a bundle or bag tied at both ends, it suggests convergence or collection, visually resembling a tied shape. This pictorial representation is historically connected to the direction 'east', as a bag captures and holds items, analogous to the rising sun being 'held' in the east. Despite alternative interpretations involving the sun and tree, the pictogram of a bundle remains the most direct visual link.
- **examples:**
  - 他的東里(裏)装(裝)满(滿)了( )书(書)。
    - Tā de dōng lǐ zhuāng mǎn le shū.
    - His bag is full of books.
  - 她( )买(買)了( )一( )个(個)新( )的( )東( )。
    - Tā mǎi le yī gè xīn de dōng.
    - She bought a new bag.
  - 在( )办(辦)公( )室( )里(裏)，他的東总(總)是( )放( )在( )椅( )子( )后(後)面( )。
    - Zài bàngōngshì lǐ, tā de dōng zǒng shì fàng zài yǐzi hòumiàn.
    - In the office, his bag is always placed behind the chair.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 東](@media/glyph6771.png)
### 动(動) → 重 → 土
- **definition:** earth
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民( )耕( )土( )，种(種)出( )丰(豐)收( )。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院( )子( )里(裡)的( )土( )，适(適)合( )种(種)花( )。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 土](@media/glyph571f.png)

## 危( )险(險)
---
## dangerous
### wēixiǎn
---
- **traditional:** 危險
- **definition:** dangerous
- **pinyin:** wēixiǎn
- **components:**
  - 危
    - wēi
    - dangerous; perilous; critical
  - 险(險)
    - xiǎn
    - perilous; risk; danger; hazard
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 危 (wēi, "dangerous") + 險 (xiǎn, "perilous; risk") =
    - the state of being prone to danger ->
    - dangerous
  - **interpretation:** 危 (wēi, "dangerous") conveys the idea of something unstable or at risk of tipping over, as seen at a cliff's edge. This visual of instability directly leads to the sense of danger. 險 (xiǎn, "perilous; risk") suggests a path or situation fraught with risk and potential for injury, such as a treacherous mountain trail. Combined, these characters evoke a sense of exposure to significant harm or risk, hence forming the concept of something being "dangerous."
- **examples:**
  - 骑(騎)车(車)没(沒)有( )戴( )头(頭)盔( )很( )危( )险(險)。
    - Qí chē méiyǒu dài tóukuī hěn wēixiǎn.
    - Riding a bike without a helmet is very dangerous.
  - 这(這)个(個)地( )区(區)晚( )上( )走( )路( )很( )危( )险(險)。
    - Zhège dìqū wǎnshàng zǒulù hěn wēixiǎn.
    - It's dangerous to walk in this area at night.
  - 他( )总(總)是( )做( )一( )些( )危( )险(險)的( )事( )情( )。
    - Tā zǒng shì zuò yīxiē wēixiǎn de shìqíng.
    - He always does some dangerous things.
### 危( )险(險) → 危
- **definition:** dangerous; perilous; critical
- **pinyin:** wēi
- **components:**
  - 懸
    - xuán
    - hanging; suspended
  - 縣
    - xiàn
    - district
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Variant form of 懸: semantic 心 ('heart') + phonetic 縣 ('district') ->
    - original meaning 'hanging; suspended'
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted the concept of something suspended or hanging, which conveys a sense of precariousness and thus 'danger'. This leads to the association with being 'high' or 'steep', as those conditions can be perilous, and more abstractly represents critical situations due to their instability.
- **examples:**
  - 那( )座( )山( )很( )危( )险(險)。
    - Nà zuò shān hěn wēixiǎn.
    - That mountain is very dangerous.
  - 这(這)座( )建( )筑(築)物( )非( )常( )危( )耸(聳)。
    - Zhè zuò jiànzhù wù fēicháng wēisǒng.
    - This building is extremely high and steep.
  - 在( )危( )急( )时(時)刻( )，他( )展( )现(現)了( )冷( )静(靜)的( )智( )慧( )。
    - Zài wēijí shíkè, tā zhǎnxiànle lěngjìng de zhìhuì.
    - In the critical moment, he showed calm wisdom.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 危](@media/glyph5371.png)
### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸
- **definition:** hanging; suspended
- **pinyin:** xuán
- **components:**
  - 縣
    - xuán
    - county
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 縣 (xuán, "county") + semantic 心 (xīn, "heart") ->
    - meaning derived from phonetic component
  - **interpretation:** The character 懸(xuán, "hang") combines the phonetic element 縣 (xuán, "county") with the semantic element 心 (xīn, "heart"). Originally, 縣 conveyed the full meaning, but 心 was added to disambiguate its meaning towards 'hang' or 'suspend' as the character evolved. Thus, 懸 signifies a sense of something hanging or being suspended metaphorically close to one's 'heart'.
  - **simplification:** Simplified as 悬: the 心 (心) (xīn, "heart") was removed for simplicity, while retaining the phonetic portion.
- **examples:**
  - 灯(燈)悬(懸)在( )天( )花( )板( )上( )。
    - Dēng xuán zài tiānhuābǎn shàng.
    - The lamp hangs from the ceiling.
  - 他( )把( )疑( )虑(慮)悬(懸)在( )心( )中( )。
    - Tā bǎ yílǜ xuán zài xīnzhōng.
    - He hangs his doubts in his heart.
  - 那( )幅( )画(畫)悬(懸)在( )墙(牆)上( )。
    - Nà fú huà xuán zài qiáng shàng.
    - The painting hangs on the wall.
### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸 → 縣
- **definition:** county
- **pinyin:** xuán
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 糸
    - sī
    - string
  - 懸
    - xuán
    - to hang
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 目 (mù, "eye/head") + 木 (mù, "tree") + 糸 (sī, "string") =
    - hanging a head by string on a tree ->
    - referred to 懸(xuán, "to hang") ->
    - later borrowed for 縣 (xuán, "county")
  - **interpretation:** The character 縣 originally depicted the head (eye) being hung by a string on a tree, symbolizing the action of hanging. This character was later borrowed for administrative divisions, likely due to the phonetic similarity to 懸(xuán, "to hang"). Over time, the original representation was adapted and corrupted, but the connotations of oversight and governance (like an overseer hanging over an area) may have influenced its adoption for 'county.'
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 縣 was simplified to 县 by removing 糸 (sī, "string") and simplifying the components for ease of writing, while retaining phonetic aspects.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )住( )在( )一( )个(個)小( )县(縣)。
    - Wǒ zhù zài yīgè xiǎo xuán.
    - I live in a small county.
  - 他( )访(訪)问(問)了( )古( )老( )的( )县(縣)，体(體)验(驗)了( )乡(鄉)村( )风(風)情( )。
    - Tā fǎngwèn le gǔlǎo de xuán, tǐyàn le xiāngcūn fēngqíng.
    - He visited an ancient county and experienced the rural customs.
  - 他( )们(們)骑(騎)车(車)穿( )过(過)县(縣)城( )，感受了悠久的文化。
    - Tāmen qí chē chuānguò xuánchéng, gǎnshòu le yōujiǔ de wénhuà.
    - They rode bicycles through the county town and experienced its long-standing culture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 縣](@media/glyph7e23.png)
### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸 → 縣 → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她( )目( )不( )转(轉)睛( )，注( )视(視)前( )方( )。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄( )鹰(鷹)展( )翅( )，双(雙)目( )炯( )炯( )看( )天( )际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.

### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸 → 縣 → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把( )椅( )子( )的( )主( )要( )材( )料( )是( )木( )。

- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )手( )工( )制(製)作( )了( )一( )条(條)漂( )亮( )的( )丝(絲)巾( )。

### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸 → 心
- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a heart
  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, "heart") originally depicted the shape of an actual heart, representing thoughts, emotions, and the core of a person. Over time, it has become highly stylized, but it continues to convey the notion of the heart as the center of emotions and consciousness.
- **examples:**
  - 她的心一( )直( )都( )在( )帮(幫)助( )别(別)人( )。
    - Tā de xīn yīzhí dōu zài bāngzhù biérén.
    - Her heart is always in helping others.
  - 在城市的中心，有( )一( )个(個)美( )丽(麗)的( )公( )园(園)。
    - Zài chéngshì de zhōngxīn, yǒu yí gè měilì de gōngyuán.
    - At the center of the city, there is a beautiful park.
  - 对(對)于(於)许(許)多( )人( )来(來)说(說)，家庭是生活的核心。
    - Duìyú xǔduō rén lái shuō, jiātíng shì shēnghuó de héxīn.
    - For many people, family is the core of life.

### 危( )险(險) → 险(險)
- **traditional:** 險
- **definition:** perilous; risk; danger; hazard
- **pinyin:** xiǎn
- **components:**
  - 阝(阜)
    - fù
    - mound
  - 僉
    - qiān
    - gather
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 阝(阜) (fù, "mound") + phonetic: 僉 (qiān) =
    - resembling a mound or high ground + phonetic value ->
    - danger or risk
  - **interpretation:** The character 險 (xiǎn, "danger") combines the element 阝(阜) (fù, "mound"), suggesting something elevated or protruding like a hill, and the phonetic 僉 (qiān), which provides the pronunciation and implies a sense of accumulation or incorporation, thus together indicating a place or situation that poses potential threat or difficulty due to its terrain or circumstances.
  - **simplification:** 險 was simplified to 险(險) by changing the left-side 阝(阜) to its common simplified form 阝(阜), while retaining the phonetic component 僉; however, 阝 represents a simplified version of the original with fewer strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )决(決)定( )冒( )险(險)一( )试(試)。
    - Tā juédìng màoxiǎn yī shì.
    - He decided to take the risk and give it a try.
  - 驾(駕)驶(駛)时(時)要( )小( )心( )，避( )免( )不( )必( )要( )的( )险(險)情( )。
    - Jiàshǐ shí yào xiǎoxīn, bìmiǎn bù bìyào de xiǎnqíng.
    - Drive carefully to avoid unnecessary dangers.
  - 探( )险(險)家( )穿( )越( )原( )始( )森( )林( )时(時)，面( )临(臨)着(著)未( )知( )的( )险(險)境( )。
    - Tànxiǎnjiā chuānyuè yuánshǐ sēnlín shí, miànlínzhe wéizhī de xiǎnjìng.
    - The explorer, while traversing the primeval forest, faced unknown hazards.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 阝
- **definition:** mound
- **pinyin:** fù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a small mound or hillock.
  - **interpretation:** The character 阝 (fù, 'mound') visually represents a small elevation of land, resembling a hillside or embankment.
- **examples:**
  - 小( )山( )顶(頂)上( )耸(聳)立( )着(著)阝(阜)。
    - Xiǎo shāndǐng shàng sǒnglì zhe fù.
    - A small mound stands atop the hill.
  - 山( )坡( )上( )长(長)满(滿)了( )绿(綠)色( )的( )草( )丛(叢)，山( )丘( )边(邊)坐( )落( )着(著)一( )座( )古( )老( )的( )阝(阜)。
    - Shānpō shàng cháng mǎn le lǜsè de cǎocóng, shānqiū biān zuòluò zhe yī zuò gǔlǎo de fù.
    - The hillside is covered with green grass, and an ancient mound sits by the hill.
  - 远(遠)处(處)沙( )丘( )边(邊)隐(隱)约(約)可( )见(見)一( )堆( )阝(阜)，仿(彷)佛(彿)历(歷)史( )的( )见(見)证(證)。
    - Yuǎnchù shāqiū biān yǐnyuē kějiàn yī duī fù, fǎngfú lìshǐ de jiànzhèng.
    - In the distance, a pile of mounds is barely visible by the sand dunes, as if witnessing history.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉
- **definition:** gather
- **pinyin:** qiān
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - jí
    - assemble
  - 兄
    - xiōng
    - elder
  - 吅
    - xuān
    - declare
  - 从
    - cóng
    - follow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 亼 (assemble) + 兄 (elder) written twice ->
    - originally depicting people responding together, stylized later as 亼 + 吅 (declare) + 从 (follow) ->
    - consensus, unanimity
  - **interpretation:** The character 僉(qiān, 'all') visually represents the idea of multiple individuals (represented by the repetition of 兄) coming together to answer or declare something as a group. This evolves into a stylization showing an assembly and group consensus, reinforcing the meaning of unanimity or all.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 僉](@media/glyph50c9.png)
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 亼
- **definition:** assemble
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 亼 → 入
- **definition:** enter
- **pinyin:** rù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** An arrowhead indicating 'to enter'
  - **interpretation:** The character 入(rù, 'enter') visually represents the concept of entering, with the form resembling an arrowhead suggesting movement through an opening.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)入( )座( )。
    - Qǐng rùzuò.
    - Please take a seat.
  - 学(學)生( )走( )入( )校( )园(園)，开(開)始( )新( )学(學)期( )。
    - Xuéshēng zǒu rù xiàoyuán, kāishǐ xīn xuéqī.
    - The students enter the campus and start a new semester.
  - 游(遊)客( )走( )入( )古( )城( )，探( )索( )历(歷)史( )。
    - Yóukè zǒu rù gǔchéng, tànsuǒ lìshǐ.
    - The tourists enter the ancient city and explore its history.

### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 亼 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )一( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他( )只( )看( )到( )一( )只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了( )花( )园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一( )条(條)直( )路( )通( )向( )远(遠)方( )。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.

### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 亼 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今( )天( )的( )天( )气(氣)不( )错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.
    - Today's weather is nice.
  - 现(現)在( )是( )吃( )晚( )饭(飯)的( )时(時)候( )。
    - Xiànzài shì chī wǎnfàn de shíhòu.
    - Now is the time to have dinner.
  - 她( )今( )天( )特( )别(別)忙( )，没(沒)时(時)间(間)见(見)面( )。
    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 亼 → 今 → 曰
- **definition:** to speak
- **pinyin:** yuē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老( )师(師)曰( )：勤( )奋(奮)是( )成( )功( )之( )母( )。
    - Lǎoshī yuē：qínfèn shì chénggōng zhī mǔ。
    - The teacher said, 'Diligence is the mother of success.'
  - 孔子曰，学(學)而( )不( )思( )则(則)罔( )。
    - Kǒngzǐ yuē, xué ér bù sī zé wǎng。
    - Confucius said, 'Learning without thought leads to confusion.'
  - 老子曰，无(無)为(為)而( )治( )。
    - Lǎozǐ yuē, wúwéi ér zhì。
    - Laozi said, 'Governance should be achieved through non-action.'

### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 兄

- **pinyin:** xiōng
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 儿
    - ér
    - child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + 儿 (ér, "child") =
    - giving orders ->
    - elder brother
  - **interpretation:** The character 兄 (xiōng, "brother") combines 口 (kǒu, "mouth") with 儿 (ér, "child") to depict an elder brother who gives orders. This conveys the traditional family role of the elder brother as a figure of authority, similar to other characters like 令 (lìng, "order") that emphasize the act of speaking or commanding.
- **examples:**

### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 兄 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.

### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 兄 → 儿(兒)
- **traditional:** 兒
- **definition:** child
- **pinyin:** ér
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an infant with an imperfect cranium (fontanelle)
  - **interpretation:** The character 兒 (ér, "child") is a pictogram representing a child with a distinctive fontanelle, highlighting the child's young age and the characteristic soft spot on the head. This reflects the character's meaning as 'child.'
  - **simplification:** 儿 is a simplified and cursive form of 兒, representing a stylistic reduction of strokes while still retaining the essence of a child's figure.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小( )女( )孩( )喜( )欢(歡)唱( )歌( )。
    - Zhè gè xiǎo nǚhái xǐhuān chànggē.

    - He has a smart son.

    - phonetic
  - **interpretation:** The character 吅(xuān, "sound; phonetic") combines two 口 (kǒu, "mouth") to symbolize the idea of multiple mouths or repeated speech, indicating sound or phonetic elements.

### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 从(從)
- **traditional:** 從
- **definition:** follow
- **pinyin:** cóng
- **components:**
  - 辵
    - chuò
    - walk; movement
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 辵 ('walk; movement') + phonetic 从 (sound) ->
    - follow
  - **interpretation:** 從 (cóng, 'to follow') combines the idea of 'walking' or 'movement' from 辵 (chuò, 'walk; movement') with the sound symbolized by 从 (cóng, 'follow'), capturing the concept of moving along a path under guidance or direction.
  - **simplification:** 从 is a variant form directly used as the simplified form, adopting the earlier, less complex writing as the standard.
- **examples:**
  - 你( )需( )要( )从(從)这(這)里(裡)开(開)始( )。
    - Nǐ xūyào cóng zhèlǐ kāishǐ.
    - You need to start from here.
  - 她( )从(從)小( )就( )喜( )欢(歡)画(畫)画(畫)。
    - Tā cóngxiǎo jiù xǐhuān huàhuà.
    - She has liked drawing since she was a child.
  - 所( )有( )东(東)西( )都( )从(從)他( )的( )袋( )子( )里(裡)掉( )出( )来(來)了( )。
    - Suǒyǒu dōngxī dōu cóng tā de dàizi lǐ diào chūláile.
    - Everything fell out of his bag.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 从](@media/glyph4ece.png)
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 从(從) → 辵
- **definition:** walk; movement
- **pinyin:** chuò
- **components:**
  - 彳
    - chì
    - walk
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 彳 (chì, "walk") + 止 (zhǐ, "foot" or "to stop") ->
    - 𣥆 ->
    - stylized as 龰 ->
    - 辵
  - **interpretation:** The character 辵 combines 彳 (chì, "walk"), which represents movement, with 止 (zhǐ, "foot" or "to stop"), suggesting the concept of stepping or traveling forward. This character represents the idea of movement, particularly the action of walking or traveling, as originally depicted by the more conservative form 𣥆. Over time, the bottom component has been stylized as 龰, forming the current representation.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )辵( )在( )乡(鄉)间(間)的( )小( )路( )上( )。
    - Tā chuò zài xiāngjiān de xiǎolù shàng.
    - He walks on the rural path.
  - 晨( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)大( )地( )，他( )辵( )出( )门(門)开(開)始( )旅( )程( )。
    - Chén guāng sǎ mǎn dàdì, tā chuò chūmén kāishǐ lǚchéng.
    - As the morning light fills the earth, he sets out to begin his journey.
- **historical forms:**

### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 从(從) → 辵 → 彳

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a foot or person walking
  - **interpretation:** 彳(chì, 'walking') visually represents steps or a person moving, suggesting the idea of walking or movement. Despite a simplified history from characters like 行(xíng, 'walk'), its pictographic heritage directly connects with the notion of stepping or proceeding.

### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 从(從) → 辵 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**

    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.

  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)的( )止( )需( )要( )静(靜)养(養)。

## 危( )险(險)

## 条(條)
---
## strip; long narrow piece; measure word for long objects
### tiáo
---
- **traditional:** 條
- **definition:** strip; long narrow piece; measure word for long objects
- **pinyin:** tiáo
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 攸
    - yōu
    - a place far away
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, "wood") + phonetic 攸 (yōu) ->
    - originally indicates a small branch or wooden stick
  - **interpretation:** The character 條 (tiáo, "strip; streak; item") combines the semantic 木 (mù, "wood") to suggest something made of wood, and the phonetic 攸 (yōu) to provide the pronunciation. Initially, it referred specifically to a small branch or stick made of wood, which logically leads to the modern extended meanings of a 'strip' or 'item' in more general contexts because of the similar shape and form.
  - **simplification:** 条(條) simplifies 條 by removing the 木 (mù, "wood") component and simplifying 攸 (yōu) to a simpler form, focusing on phonetics rather than semantic resemblance to wood.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)条(條)裙( )子( )很( )好( )看( )。
    - Zhè tiáo qúnzi hěn hǎokàn.
    - This dress looks very nice.
  - 河( )上( )架( )了( )一( )座( )长(長)长(長)的( )桥(橋)。
    - Hé shàng jiàle yī zuò cháng cháng de qiáo.
    - A long bridge was built over the river.
  - 他( )发(發)送( )了( )一( )条(條)短( )信( )，通( )知( )朋( )友( )聚( )会(會)时(時)间(間)。
    - Tā fāsòngle yī tiáo duǎnxìn, tōngzhī péngyǒu jùhuì shíjiān.
    - He sent a text message, informing friends of the gathering time.
### 条(條) → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把( )椅( )子( )的( )主( )要( )材( )料( )是( )木( )。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
### 条(條) → 攸
- **definition:** a place far away
- **pinyin:** yōu
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 攴
    - pū
    - strike
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 攴 (pū, "strike" or "hit") ->
    - depiction may include drops of water ->
    - combines to suggest 'warning' or 'purification'
  - **interpretation:** The character 攸 is an ideogrammic compound with 人 (rén, "person") + 攴 (pū, "strike" or "hit"). Two interpretations exist: one posits it as a depiction of a person about to be disciplined, thus suggesting 'warning'; another suggests a ritual washing, connected to ceremonial purification, and thus involves water symbolism. The sense of 'distant' likely emerged as a metaphorical extension from the idea of warning or cleansing, which sets one apart or corrects a path.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 攸](@media/glyph6538.png)
### 条(條) → 攸 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )个(個)好( )人( )。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每( )个(個)人( )都( )有( )责(責)任( )，为(為)社( )会(會)作( )出( )贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心( )灵(靈)获(獲)得( )了( )成( )长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.

### 条(條) → 攸 → 攴
- **definition:** strike
- **pinyin:** pū
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, 'hand') depicted as 又 (yòu, 'hand') holding a tool ->
    - later stylized to look like 卜 (bǔ, 'divine') ->
    - simplified further
  - **interpretation:** The character 攴 originally depicted a hand holding a tool, possibly implying action such as hitting. Over time, for stylistic reasons, it was modified to resemble the component 卜, even though the phonetic aspect was retained.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手指攴轻(輕)叩( )鼓( )面( )，传(傳)递(遞)出( )节(節)奏( )的( )信( )号(號)。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ pū le qīng kòu gǔmiàn, chuándì chū jiézòu de xìnhào.
    - He tapped the drum surface lightly with his finger, conveying the rhythm's signal.
  - 她突然攴了( )一( )下( )门(門)，唤(喚)起( )了( )室( )内(內)的( )安( )静(靜)。
    - Tā túrán pū le yīxià mén, huànqǐ le shìnèi de ānjìng.
    - She suddenly tapped the door, awakening the quiet inside.

### 条(條) → 攸 → 攴 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )手( )写(寫)字( )。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.

    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他( )的( )手( )很( )温(溫)暖( )，带(帶)给(給)我( )力( )量( )。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.

### 条(條) → 攸 → 攴 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又( )」这(這)个(個)字( )最( )早( )来(來)源( )于(於)手( )。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很( )多( )汉(漢)字( )含( )有( )又( )部( )首( )，表( )示( )与(與)手( )有( )关(關)的( )动(動)作( )。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古( )人( )用( )又( )描( )绘(繪)手( )的( )形( )态(態)，体(體)现(現)了( )古( )汉(漢)字( )的( )独(獨)特( )魅( )力( )。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.

### 条(條) → 攸 → 攴 → 卜
- **definition:** divine
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人( )们(們)常( )用( )龟(龜)甲( )进(進)行( )卜( )卦( )。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他( )对(對)未( )来(來)充( )满(滿)疑( )虑(慮)，所( )以( )决(決)定( )找( )人( )卜( )卦( )。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在( )占( )星( )术(術)中( )，卜( )法( )常( )被( )用( )来(來)预(預)测(測)未( )来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.
- **historical forms:**

## 龙(龍)
---
## dragon
### lóng
---
- **traditional:** 龍
- **definition:** dragon
- **pinyin:** lóng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally depicted a serpent with a prominent whiskered mouth and eyes ->
    - large seal script developed into a dragon's body ->
    - simplified abstraction influenced by 立 (lì, "stand") and ⺼ (ròu, "flesh")
  - **interpretation:** The traditional character 龍(lóng, "dragon") began as a pictogram illustrating a serpent's key features, particularly its whiskered mouth and eyes, fundamental to the cultural depiction of dragons as mythical creatures with such traits. Despite changes and simplifications over time, this form has retained its original essence within the body and structural elements adapted over centuries, evidencing a complex fusion of visual components and cultural evolution.
  - **simplification:** The character 龙 is a simplified version of the traditional 龍, where the intricate elements were streamlined by removing sections like 帝 and simplifying 彡, reducing the complexity for easier writing.
- **examples:**
  - 龙(龍)是( )中( )国(國)文( )化( )的( )重( )要( )象( )征(徵)。
    - Lóng shì Zhōngguó wénhuà de zhòngyào xiàngzhēng.
    - The dragon is an important symbol in Chinese culture.
  - 舞( )龙(龍)是( )春( )节(節)的( )传(傳)统(統)活( )动(動)。
    - Wǔlóng shì Chūnjié de chuántǒng huódòng.
    - Dragon dance is a traditional activity during the Spring Festival.
  - 皇( )帝( )被( )称(稱)为(為)真( )龙(龍)天( )子( )。
    - Huángdì bèi chēng wéi zhēnlóng tiānzǐ.
    - The emperor was called the true dragon son of heaven.

## 拍
---
## to pat; to beat; to take (a picture)
### pāi
---
- **definition:** to pat; to beat; to take (a picture)
- **pinyin:** pāi
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 白
    - bái
    - white
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 扌(手) (shǒu, "hand") + phonetic 白 (bái, "white") ->
    - hand action ->
    - to pat; to beat
  - **interpretation:** 拍(pāi, "to pat; to beat; to take (a picture)") combines the semantic component 扌(手) (shǒu, "hand"), indicating movement or using the hand, with the phonetic component 白 (bái). The action of a hand repeatedly contacting a surface naturally conveys the sense of 'pat' or 'beat'. This character was adapted for the meaning 'to take (a picture)' as taking a photograph is a rapid capturing process similar to a pat.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )轻(輕)轻(輕)地( )拍( )他( )的( )肩( )膀( )。
    - Tā qīngqīng de pāi tā de jiānbǎng.
    - He lightly patted his shoulder.
  - 我( )今( )天( )拍( )了( )一( )张(張)很( )漂( )亮( )的( )照( )片( )。
    - Wǒ jīntiān pāi le yī zhāng hěn piàoliang de zhàopiàn.
    - I took a very beautiful picture today.
  - 摄(攝)影( )师(師)在( )公( )园(園)拍( )风(風)景( )照( )片( )。
    - Shèyǐngshī zài gōngyuán pāi fēngjǐng zhàopiàn.
    - The photographer takes landscape photos in the park.
### 拍 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )手( )写(寫)字( )。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我( )的( )手( )走( )路( )。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他( )的( )手( )很( )温(溫)暖( )，带(帶)给(給)我( )力( )量( )。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 拍 → 白
- **definition:** white
- **pinyin:** bái
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts an acorn ->
    - white from the color of acorn's inside
  - **interpretation:** The character 白(bái, "white") is thought to depict an acorn, as suggested by its use in words related to oak and acorns. The character's meaning of "white" is likely derived from the white color of an acorn's interior.
- **examples:**
  - 白( )色( )是( )我( )最( )喜( )欢(歡)的( )颜(顏)色( )。
    - Báisè shì wǒ zuì xǐhuān de yánsè.
    - White is my favorite color.
  - 他( )的( )头(頭)发(髮)已( )经(經)全( )白( )了( )。
    - Tā de tóufà yǐjīng quán bái le.
    - His hair has turned completely white.
  - 在( )阳(陽)光( )下( )，白( )沙( )滩(灘)显(顯)得( )格( )外( )美( )丽(麗)。
    - Zài yángguāng xià, bái shātān xiǎnde géwài měilì.
    - In the sunlight, the white sandy beach looks especially beautiful.
- **historical forms:**

## 秋天
---
## autumn
### qiūtiān
---
- **definition:** autumn
- **pinyin:** qiūtiān
- **components:**
  - 秋
    - qiū
    - autumn
  - 天
    - tiān
    - sky; heaven; weather
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 秋 (qiū, "autumn") + 天 (tiān, "sky; heaven; weather") combine to mean "autumn". In this context, the characters suggest the 'autumn season', linking the time of year (秋) with the general concept of time or weather (天).
  - **interpretation:** 秋 (qiū, "autumn") represents the season following summer, characterized by harvest time. 天 (tiān, "sky; heaven; weather") commonly denotes weather or a period in general. The term 秋天 expresses the particular segment of time within a year designated as autumn, combining the notion of this transitional period with its atmospheric and temporal nuances that 天 implies.
- **examples:**
  - 秋( )天( )是( )一( )个(個)收( )获(穫)的( )季( )节(節)。
    - Qiūtiān shì yī ge shōuhuò de jìjié.
    - Autumn is a season of harvest.
  - 秋天到了，树(樹)叶(葉)变(變)成( )了( )金( )黄(黃)色( )。
    - Qiūtiān dào le, shùyè biàn chéng le jīnhuángsè.
    - Autumn has arrived, and the leaves have turned golden yellow.
  - 在秋天，我( )们(們)常( )去( )公( )园(園)散( )步( )。
    - Zài qiūtiān, wǒmen cháng qù gōngyuán sànbù.
    - In autumn, we often go for walks in the park.
### 秋天 → 秋
- **definition:** autumn
- **pinyin:** qiū
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 禾 (hé, 'grain') + 火 (huǒ, 'fire') =
    - grain + fire ->
    - harvest time ->
    - autumn
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 'grain' and 'fire', symbolizing the practice of burning fields after harvest, marking autumn as harvest time.
- **examples:**
  - 秋( )天( )来(來)了( )。
    - Qiū tiān lái le.
    - Autumn has arrived.
  - 秋( )风(風)送( )爽( )，稻( )谷(穀)金( )黄(黃)。
    - Qiū fēng sòng shuǎng, dào gǔ jīn huáng.
    - The autumn breeze brings coolness, and the rice is golden.
  - 在秋季的午后，书(書)香( )满(滿)室( )。
    - Zài qiū jì de wǔ hòu, shū xiāng mǎn shì.
    - On an autumn afternoon, the room is filled with the fragrance of books.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 秋](@media/glyph79cb.png)
### 秋天 → 秋 → 禾
- **definition:** grain
- **pinyin:** hé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stalk of grain or cereal plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 禾 (hé, 'grain') visually represents a plant with roots and leaves, focusing on the appearance of staple crops like rice or millet. This clearly conveys its meaning as it resembles the actual shape of a plant grown for its grain.
- **examples:**
  - 收( )获(穫)的( )禾( )香( )弥(彌)漫( )在( )田( )野( )中( )。

    - The hardworking farmers harvested the ears of grain.
  - 春( )雨( )滋( )润(潤)了( )禾( )苗( )，预(預)示( )着(著)丰(豐)收( )。
    - Chūnyǔ zīrùn le hé miáo, yùshì zhe fēngshōu.
    - The spring rain nourished the grain seedlings, foreshadowing a bountiful harvest.

### 秋天 → 秋 → 火
- **definition:** fire
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames rising from a fire
  - **interpretation:** The character 火 (huǒ, "fire") visually represents flames flickering upwards, which intuitively conveys the essence of fire. This simple depiction is an effective way to capture the dynamic and essential nature of fire.
- **examples:**
  - 火( )在( )壁( )炉(爐)中( )熊( )熊( )燃( )烧(燒)。

    - Yěwài lùyíng shí, huǒ néng qūzǒu hánlěng.
    - When camping outdoors, the fire can drive away the cold.
  - 遇( )到( )火( )灾(災)时(時)，迅( )速( )疏( )散( )最( )为(為)重( )要( )。
    - Yù dào huǒzāi shí, xùnsù shū sàn zuìwéi zhòngyào.

### 秋天 → 天
- **definition:** sky; heaven; weather
- **pinyin:** tiān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horizontal line above 大(dà, "big") to depict sky ->
    - anthropomorphic man with large head symbolizing heaven
  - **interpretation:** The character 天(tiān) originally depicts the sky as a horizontal line above a person with outstretched arms, 大(dà, "big"), emphasizing the vastness or domain of heaven. Over time, the character evolved into an anthropomorphic representation of heaven, which later influenced its interpretation in classical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 夜( )幕( )降( )临(臨)，天( )边(邊)星( )光( )闪(閃)烁(爍)。
    - Yèmù jiànglín, tiānbiān xīnguāng shǎnshuò.
    - As night falls, starlight gleams on the horizon.
  - 他仰望高空，祈( )求( )天( )佑( )众(眾)生( )。
    - Tā yǎngwàng gāokōng, qíqiú tiānyòu zhòngshēng.
    - He gazes up to the sky and prays for heaven's protection over all living beings.
- **historical forms:**

## 阴(陰)天( )
---
## cloudy sky; overcast weather
### yīntiān
---
- **traditional:** 陰天
- **definition:** cloudy sky; overcast weather
- **pinyin:** yīntiān
- **components:**
  - 阴(陰)
    - yīn
    - cloudy; negative; hidden
  - 天
    - tiān
    - sky; heaven; day
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 陰 (yīn, "cloudy; negative; hidden") indicates cloudy or shadowed conditions, as it typically represents the shaded or obscure side of a hill, metaphorically linked to overcast weather; 天 (tiān, "sky; heaven; day") is the sky or celestial space, relating to the weather above us.
  - **interpretation:** 陰 (yīn, "cloudy; hidden") conveys shadowy or overcast weather, implying the presence of clouds that obscure sunlight; it also connotes negativity as clouds can bring gloom. 天 (tiān, "sky") naturally represents the weather or atmosphere, so 阴(陰)天( ) (yīntiān) literally combines these to signify 'cloudy sky' or 'overcast weather', as a sky shadowed by clouds blocking the sun's light.
- **examples:**
  - 今( )天( )是( )阴(陰)天( )。
    - Jīntiān shì yīntiān.
    - Today is cloudy.
  - 阴(陰)天( )的( )时(時)候( )，我( )喜( )欢(歡)喝( )热(熱)茶( )。
    - Yīntiān de shíhòu, wǒ xǐhuān hē rè chá.
    - When it's cloudy, I like to drink hot tea.
  - 阴(陰)天( )让(讓)人( )感( )觉(覺)很( )放( )松(鬆)。
    - Yīntiān ràng rén gǎnjué hěn fàngsōng.
    - Cloudy weather makes people feel relaxed.
### 阴(陰)天( ) → 阴(陰)
- **traditional:** 陰
- **definition:** cloudy; negative; hidden
- **pinyin:** yīn
- **components:**
  - 阜
    - fù
    - mound
  - 侌
    - yīn
    - concealed
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 阜 (fù, "mound") + phonetic 侌 (yīn, "concealed") ->
    - concealed location ->
    - shade, moon, female
  - **interpretation:** The character 陰 (yīn, "concealed; shade; moon; female") combines 阜 (fù, "mound") suggesting a hill or elevation that blocks light, with 侌 (yīn, "concealed") indicating the hidden or shadowy aspect of such a place. Together, they convey the concept of something being hidden in the shadow of a hill or mound, thus connecting to ideas of shade and concealment. The association with the moon and female stems from the moon's own phases of visibility and its yin-feminine qualities in Chinese philosophy.
  - **simplification:** An unorthodox variant where 侌 (yīn, "concealed") was replaced with the component 月 (yuè, "moon") was eventually adopted as the official simplified form in 1956.
- **examples:**
  - 天( )气(氣)阴(陰)沉( )，似乎要下雨。
    - Tiānqì yīnchén, sìhū yào xiàyǔ.
    - The weather is gloomy, it seems like it's going to rain.
  - 她( )走( )进(進)了( )阴(陰)影( )里(裡)，消( )失( )不( )见(見)。
    - Tā zǒu jìnle yīnyǐng lǐ, xiāoshī bùjiàn.
    - She walked into the shadow and disappeared.
  - 月( )亮( )只( )有( )半( )边(邊)在( )夜( )空( )中( )显(顯)示( )。
    - Yuèliang zhǐyǒu bànbiān zài yèkōng zhōng xiǎnshì.
    - Only half of the moon is visible in the night sky.

- **pinyin:** fù
- **etymology:**

  - **interpretation:** The character 阜 (fù, "mound") originally depicted the silhouette of a small hill or mound, representing its natural shape and structure.
- **examples:**
  - 山( )边(邊)的( )小( )阜( )上( )，盛( )开(開)着(著)野( )花( )。
    - Shān biān de xiǎo fù shàng, shèng kāi zhe yě huā.
    - Wildflowers bloom atop the small mound by the mountainside.
  - 古( )道( )尽(盡)头(頭)有( )阜( )。

### 阴(陰)天( ) → 阴(陰) → 侌 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今( )天( )的( )天( )气(氣)不( )错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.

    - Now is the time to have dinner.

    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 阴(陰)天( ) → 阴(陰) → 侌 → 今 → 曰
- **definition:** to speak
- **pinyin:** yuē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老( )师(師)曰( )：勤( )奋(奮)是( )成( )功( )之( )母( )。

  - 孔子曰，学(學)而( )不( )思( )则(則)罔( )。

    - Confucius said, 'Learning without thought leads to confusion.'
  - 老子曰，无(無)为(為)而( )治( )。

    - Laozi said, 'Governance should be achieved through non-action.'

### 阴(陰)天( ) → 阴(陰) → 侌 → 今 → 亼
- **definition:** collect; assemble
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)
### 阴(陰)天( ) → 阴(陰) → 侌 → 今 → 亼 → 入
- **definition:** enter
- **pinyin:** rù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** An arrowhead indicating 'to enter'
  - **interpretation:** The character 入(rù, 'enter') visually represents the concept of entering, with the form resembling an arrowhead suggesting movement through an opening.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)入( )座( )。
    - Qǐng rùzuò.
    - Please take a seat.
  - 学(學)生( )走( )入( )校( )园(園)，开(開)始( )新( )学(學)期( )。
    - Xuéshēng zǒu rù xiàoyuán, kāishǐ xīn xuéqī.
    - The students enter the campus and start a new semester.
  - 游(遊)客( )走( )入( )古( )城( )，探( )索( )历(歷)史( )。
    - Yóukè zǒu rù gǔchéng, tànsuǒ lìshǐ.
    - The tourists enter the ancient city and explore its history.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 入](@media/glyph5165.png)
### 阴(陰)天( ) → 阴(陰) → 侌 → 今 → 亼 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )一( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他( )只( )看( )到( )一( )只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了( )花( )园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一( )条(條)直( )路( )通( )向( )远(遠)方( )。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.

### 阴(陰)天( ) → 天
- **definition:** sky; heaven; day
- **pinyin:** tiān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horizontal line above 大(dà, "big") to depict sky ->
    - anthropomorphic man with large head symbolizing heaven
  - **interpretation:** The character 天(tiān) originally depicts the sky as a horizontal line above a person with outstretched arms, 大(dà, "big"), emphasizing the vastness or domain of heaven. Over time, the character evolved into an anthropomorphic representation of heaven, which later influenced its interpretation in classical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 夜( )幕( )降( )临(臨)，天( )边(邊)星( )光( )闪(閃)烁(爍)。
    - Yèmù jiànglín, tiānbiān xīnguāng shǎnshuò.
    - As night falls, starlight gleams on the horizon.
  - 他仰望高空，祈( )求( )天( )佑( )众(眾)生( )。
    - Tā yǎngwàng gāokōng, qíqiú tiānyòu zhòngshēng.
    - He gazes up to the sky and prays for heaven's protection over all living beings.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 天](@media/glyph5929.png)

## 下雪
---
## to snow
### xià xuě
---
- **definition:** to snow
- **pinyin:** xià xuě
- **components:**
  - 下
    - xià
    - down
  - 雪
    - xuě
    - snow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 下 (xià, "down") + 雪 (xuě, "snow")
  - **interpretation:** 下 (xià, "down") describes the direction in which snow falls, as it comes from the sky above. 雪 (xuě, "snow") refers to the frozen precipitation that falls during winter. Together, these parts describe the action of snow falling from the sky, hence 'to snow'.
- **examples:**
  - 冬天常常下雪。
    - Dōngtiān chángcháng xià xuě.
    - It often snows in winter.
  - 昨晚下雪了，早( )上( )地( )上( )有( )一( )层(層)雪( )。
    - Zuówǎn xià xuě le, zǎoshang dìshàng yǒu yī céng xuě.
    - It snowed last night, and there is a layer of snow on the ground this morning.
  - 如( )果( )晚( )上( )还(還)下( )雪( )，我( )们(們)明( )天( )就( )去( )滑( )雪( )。
    - Rúguǒ wǎnshàng hái xià xuě, wǒmen míngtiān jiù qù huáxuě.
    - If it continues to snow tonight, we'll go skiing tomorrow.
### 下雪 → 下
- **definition:** down
- **pinyin:** xià
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - a line below another ->
    - later evolved into 下
  - **interpretation:** The character 下(xià, 'down') is an ideogram showing a line positioned below another line, visually representing 'below' or 'downward'. This layout intuitively depicts the concept of being beneath or beneath another object.
- **examples:**
  - 水( )从(從)山( )上( )流( )下( )。
    - Shuǐ cóng shān shàng liú xià.
    - The water flows down from the mountain.
  - 他( )坐( )下( )来(來)看( )书(書)。
    - Tā zuò xià lái kàn shū.
    - He sits down to read a book.
  - 请(請)把( )箱( )子( )放( )在( )地( )下( )。
    - Qǐng bǎ xiāngzi fàng zài dìxià.
    - Please put the box down on the ground.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 下](@media/glyph4e0b.png)
### 下雪 → 雪
- **definition:** snow
- **pinyin:** xuě
- **components:**
  - 雨
    - yǔ
    - rain
  - 彗
    - huì
    - broom
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 雨 (yǔ, "rain") + phonetic 彗 (huì, "broom") ->
    - snow
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 雨 (yǔ, "rain") for the semantic idea of precipitation and 彗 (huì, "broom") for its phonetic value. The image of rain light and fluffy as a broom sweep implies the specific type of precipitation: snow.
- **examples:**
  - 冬( )天( )的( )时(時)候( )，我( )们(們)经(經)常( )去( )山( )上( )滑( )雪( )。
    - Dōngtiān de shíhòu, wǒmen jīngcháng qù shānshàng huáxuě.
    - In winter, we often go to the mountains to ski.
  - 昨天晚上下了很多雪。
    - Zuótiān wǎnshàng xiàle hěnduō xuě.
    - It snowed a lot last night.
  - 雪( )花( )在( )阳(陽)光( )下( )闪(閃)闪(閃)发(發)光( )。
    - Xuěhuā zài yángguāng xià shǎnshǎn fāguāng.
    - The snowflakes sparkle under the sunlight.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 雪](@media/glyph96ea.png)
### 下雪 → 雪 → 雨
- **definition:** rain
- **pinyin:** yǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a cloud with drops of rain falling from it ->
    - horizontal stroke added later ->
    - rain
  - **interpretation:** 雨 (yǔ, "rain") visually represents rain falling from a cloud, capturing its essential form.
- **examples:**
  - 今天雨下得很大。
    - Jīntiān yǔ xià de hěn dà.
    - It rained hard today.
  - 他( )忘( )记(記)带(帶)伞(傘)，雨( )却(卻)毫( )不( )留( )情( )。
    - Tā wàngjì dài sǎn, yǔ què háobù liúqíng.
    - He forgot to bring an umbrella, and the rain showed no mercy.
  - 细(細)雨( )如( )丝(絲)，轻(輕)拂( )着(著)花( )瓣( )。
    - Xì yǔ rú sī, qīng fú zhe huā bàn.
    - The fine rain falls like silk, gently brushing the petals.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 雨](@media/glyph96e8.png)
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗
- **definition:** broom
- **pinyin:** huì
- **components:**
  - 甡
    - shēn
    - broom
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 甡 (shēn, "broom") + 又 (yòu, "hand") =
    - holding a broom
  - **interpretation:** The character 彗 (huì, "broom") combines 甡 (shēn, "broom") with 又 (yòu, "hand") to depict the action of holding a broom. This emphasizes the function and use of a broom, suggesting an object specifically designed to be held by hand for sweeping.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )拿( )着(著)破( )旧(舊)的( )彗( )，清( )扫(掃)庭( )院( )。
    - Tā ná zhe pò jiù de huì, qīng sǎo tíng yuàn.
    - He holds the old broom and sweeps the courtyard.
  - 老匠人用彗，细(細)致(緻)打( )扫(掃)作( )坊( )。
    - Lǎo jiàngrén yòng huì, xìzhì dǎsǎo zuòfāng.
    - The old craftsman uses the broom to meticulously clean the workshop.
  - 在寒冬夜晚，他默默拿起彗，清( )扫(掃)门(門)前( )。
    - Zài hán dōng yè wǎn, tā mò mò ná qǐ huì, qīng sǎo mén qián.
    - On a cold winter night, he silently picked up the broom and swept the front door.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 彗](@media/glyph5f57.png)
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗 → 甡
- **definition:** broom
- **pinyin:** shēn
- **components:**
  - 生
    - shēng
    - life
  - 辛
    - xīn
    - bitter; toilsome
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 生 (shēng, "life") + phonetic 辛 (xīn) ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** The character 甡 contains the semantic component 生 (shēng, "life") which may suggest something related to production or generation, combined with the phonetic 辛 (xīn), which contributes the sound. The character's connection to 'broom' is through borrowing for phonetic purposes and does not derive directly from its parts.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 甡](@media/glyph7521.png)
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗 → 甡 → 生
- **definition:** life
- **pinyin:** shēng
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 屮 (chè, "sprout") on top of a horizontal line ->
    - signifies a plant sprouting from the ground ->
    - symbolizes life
  - **interpretation:** The character 生 (shēng, "life") represents the concept of life force or vitality, symbolized by a sprout emerging from the earth, embodying growth and renewal.
- **examples:**
  - 生( )命( )是( )一( )场(場)美( )丽(麗)的( )旅( )程( )。
    - Shēngmìng shì yī chǎng měilì de lǚchéng.
    - Life is a beautiful journey.
  - 他( )在( )战(戰)场(場)上( )奋(奮)力( )生( )存( )。
    - Tā zài zhànchǎng shàng fènlì shēngcún.
    - He fights to live on the battlefield.
  - 这(這)家( )餐( )厅(廳)的( )生( )鱼(魚)片( )非( )常( )新( )鲜(鮮)。
    - Zhè jiā cāntīng de shēngyúpiàn fēicháng xīnxiān.
    - The raw fish slices at this restaurant are very fresh.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 生](@media/glyph751f.png)
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗 → 甡 → 生 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春( )雨( )滋( )润(潤)后(後)，小( )屮( )冲(沖)破( )泥( )土( )而( )出( )。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 屮](@media/glyph5c6e.png)
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗 → 甡 → 辛
- **definition:** bitter; toilsome
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a tool—chisel or awl—used to mark slaves and criminals ->
    - 辛
  - **interpretation:** The character 辛 (xīn) originally depicted a tool such as a chisel, used for marking or branding. The association with a sharp tool helps explain its extended meaning of 'spice,' as spices can have a pungent, sharp quality reminiscent of a tool's point or effect.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)菜( )有( )一( )种(種)辛( )辣( )的( )味( )道( )。
    - Zhège cài yǒu yī zhǒng xīnlà de wèidào.
    - This dish has a spicy taste.
  - 他( )喜( )欢(歡)在( )食( )物( )里(裡)添( )加( )辛( )香( )料( )。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài shíwù lǐ tiānjiā xīn xiāngliào.
    - He likes to add spices to the food.
  - 这(這)种(種)辛( )口( )的( )调(調)料( )非( )常( )受( )欢(歡)迎( )。
    - Zhè zhǒng xīnkǒu de tiáoliào fēicháng shòu huānyíng.
    - This type of spicy seasoning is very popular.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 辛](@media/glyph8f9b.png)
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又( )」这(這)个(個)字( )最( )早( )来(來)源( )于(於)手( )。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很( )多( )汉(漢)字( )含( )有( )又( )部( )首( )，表( )示( )与(與)手( )有( )关(關)的( )动(動)作( )。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古( )人( )用( )又( )描( )绘(繪)手( )的( )形( )态(態)，体(體)现(現)了( )古( )汉(漢)字( )的( )独(獨)特( )魅( )力( )。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**
